}) .map(function(student) { return sanitizeStudentForRole_(student, admin); }); return jsonOutput_({ status: "success", admin, students, count: students.length, source: "학생명단", message: "전체 학생명단에서 " + students.length + "명을 불러왔습니다." }); } const students = scanAttendanceClassRoster_(classQuery, keyword, admin) .map(function(student) { return sanitizeStudentForRole_(student, admin); }); return jsonOutput_({ status: "success", admin, students, count: students.length, source: "출석부 현재반", message: "출석부 현재반 기준으로 " + students.length + "명을 불러왔습니다." }); } catch (err) { return jsonOutput_({ status: "error", message: err.message }); } } function scanAttendanceClassRoster_(classQuery, keyword, admin) { const attendanceSS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID); const students = getStudentsForAdmin_(); const studentMap = {}; students.forEach(function(student) { if (student && student.nameKey) studentMap[student.nameKey] = student; }); const rows = []; const seen = {}; attendanceSS.getSheets().forEach(function(sheet) { const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (sheetName === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록)/.test(sheetName)) return; if (!sheetCouldContainClassQuery_(sheetName, classQuery)) return; const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); if (!classBelongsToAdmin_(classQuery, teacher, admin)) return; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 220); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 26); if (lastRow < 5 || lastCol < 2) return; const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getDisplayValues(); const panels = getAttendanceMonthPanelsForDate_(values, { valid: false }); panels.forEach(function(panel) { const classCells = findMatchingClassCellsInPanel_(values, panel, teacher, classQuery); classCells.forEach(function(classCell) { const nameHeader = findNameHeaderBelowClassCell_(values, classCell.row, panel); if (!nameHeader) return; const dayText = findDayTextAroundClassCell_(values, classCell.row, panel) || findDayTextInAttendancePanel_(values, nameHeader.row, panel); const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, classCell.classText); const instructor = normalizeTeacherAlias_(teacher.replace(/T$/, ""), false); if (!attendanceClassQueryMatchesRecord_(classQuery, { className: className, instructor: instructor })) return; const endRow = findStudentBlockEndAfterHeader_(values, nameHeader.row, panel); for (let r = nameHeader.row + 1; r <= endRow && r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const nameText = String(row[nameHeader.col] || row[panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); if (!isNameCellLikeStudent_(nameText)) continue; const nameKey = normalizeName(nameText); const base = studentMap[nameKey] || makeFallbackStudent_(nameText, instructor); const merged = Object.assign({}, base, { name: base.name || nameText, studentName: base.name || nameText, nameKey: nameKey, instructor: normalizeTeacherAlias_(base.instructor || instructor, false), instructorName: normalizeTeacherAlias_(base.instructor || instructor, false), className: className, currentClass: className, memo: base.memo || "", source: "출석부 " + sheetName }); if (!studentBelongsToAdmin_(merged, admin)) continue; if (!studentKeywordMatchesForClassRoster_(merged, keyword)) continue; const key = [normalizeForLooseMatch_(className), nameKey].join("|"); if (!seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; rows.push(merged); } } }); }); }); rows.sort(function(a, b) { return [a.instructor, a.className, a.name].join("|") .localeCompare([b.instructor, b.className, b.name].join("|"), "ko"); }); return rows; } function studentKeywordMatchesForClassRoster_(student, keyword) { const key = normalizeForLooseMatch_(keyword || "").toLowerCase(); if (!key) return true; const blob = normalizeForLooseMatch_([ student && (student.name || student.studentName), student && student.studentNo, student && student.studentPhone, student && student.parentPhone, student && student.instructor, student && student.className, student && student.currentClass, student && student.memo ].join(" ")).toLowerCase(); return blob.indexOf(key) !== -1; } /**************************************************** * 관리자 출석부 고정 구조 파서 v17 * - 월 패널: 5월 B:H / 6월 J:P처럼 월 제목이 있는 패널만 읽음 * - 학생명: 각 패널의 이름 열(C/K 등) * - 출결: 이름 오른쪽 날짜 열(D~G / L~O 등) * - 메모: 각 패널의 비고 열(H/P 등) * - 색상: 이름 칸 또는 해당 날짜 칸의 배경색 ****************************************************/ function getAttendanceMonthPanelsForDate_(values, dateInfo) { const defaultPanels = [ { start: 1, end: 7, noCol: 1, nameCol: 2, memoCol: 7 }, // B:H { start: 9, end: 15, noCol: 9, nameCol: 10, memoCol: 15 } // J:P ]; if (!dateInfo || !dateInfo.valid) return defaultPanels; const monthNames = [Number(dateInfo.mm) + "월", dateInfo.mm2 + "월"]; const active = []; const scanRows = Math.min(values.length, 12); defaultPanels.forEach(function(panel) { let found = false; for (let r = 0; r < scanRows; r++) { for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < (values[r] || []).length; c++) { const text = String((values[r] || [])[c] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (monthNames.indexOf(text) !== -1) { found = true; break; } } if (found) break; } if (found) active.push(panel); }); // 월 제목을 못 찾는 특수 시트에서도 기능이 죽지 않도록 마지막 fallback. return active.length ? active : defaultPanels; } function attendancePanelContainsCol_(panel, col) { return panel && col >= panel.start && col <= panel.end; } function getPanelForNameCol_(panels, nameCol) { for (let i = 0; i < panels.length; i++) { if (attendancePanelContainsCol_(panels[i], nameCol)) return panels[i]; } return null; } function buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_(values, sheetName, dateInfo) { const blocks = []; const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); const panels = getAttendanceMonthPanelsForDate_(values, dateInfo); const targetWeekday = dateInfo && dateInfo.weekday ? String(dateInfo.weekday).trim() : ""; for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) { if (normalizeHeader_(row[c]) !== "이름") continue; const panel = getPanelForNameCol_(panels, c); if (!panel) continue; // v93: 오늘 요일 블록만 먼저 통과시킵니다. // 예: 오늘이 월요일이면 출석부 3열/17열...의 "월요일" 블록만 조회합니다. // 오늘 날짜가 있더라도 토/일요일 블록은 절대 후보에 넣지 않습니다. const dayText = findDayTextInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel); if (!dayText || (targetWeekday && dayText !== targetWeekday)) continue; const dateCol = findDateColumnInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel, dateInfo); if (dateCol < 0) continue; const classText = findClassTextInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel); if (!classText) continue; blocks.push({ sheetName, teacher, panel, headerRow: r, blockEnd: findStudentBlockEndAfterHeader_(values, r, panel), nameCol: c, dateCol, memoCol: panel.memoCol, dayText, classText }); } } return blocks; } function findDateColumnInAttendancePanel_(values, headerRow, panel, dateInfo) { if (!dateInfo || !dateInfo.valid) return -1; const startRow = Math.max(0, headerRow - 1); const endRow = Math.min(values.length - 1, headerRow + 1); const startCol = panel.nameCol + 1; const endCol = panel.memoCol - 1; for (let r = endRow; r >= startRow; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = startCol; c <= endCol && c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!text) continue; // v93: 날짜는 월/일이 함께 있는 형태만 인정합니다. // "1주차"의 1, "2주차"의 2 같은 숫자만으로는 절대 매칭하지 않습니다. if (dateInfo.patterns.indexOf(text) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "/" + dateInfo.dd) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm2 + "/" + dateInfo.dd2) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "." + dateInfo.dd) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm2 + "." + dateInfo.dd2) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "월" + dateInfo.dd + "일") !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm2 + "월" + dateInfo.dd2 + "일") !== -1) return c; } } return -1; } function findClassTextInAttendancePanel_(values, headerRow, panel) { let best = null; const startRow = Math.max(0, headerRow - 7); const endRow = Math.max(0, headerRow - 1); for (let r = endRow; r >= startRow; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = cleanClassCellText_(row[c]); if (!isAttendanceClassCellText_(text)) continue; const score = Math.abs(c - panel.nameCol) + Math.abs(r - headerRow) * 3; if (!best || score < best.score) best = { text, score }; } } return best ? best.text : ""; } function findDayTextInAttendancePanel_(values, headerRow, panel) { const weekdays = ["월요일", "화요일", "수요일", "목요일", "금요일", "토요일", "일요일"]; const startRow = Math.max(0, headerRow - 9); const endRow = Math.max(0, headerRow - 1); for (let r = endRow; r >= startRow; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").trim(); if (weekdays.indexOf(text) !== -1) return text; } } return ""; } function isNameCellLikeStudent_(nameText) { const nameKey = normalizeName(nameText); if (!nameKey) return false; if (/^(이름|출석현황|수업내용|비고|NO)$/i.test(nameText)) return false; return /^[가-힣A-Za-z0-9]{2,20}$/.test(nameKey); } function getPanelMemo_(row, panel) { return String((row || [])[panel.memoCol] || "").trim(); } function adminGetClassList_(params) { try { const admin = requireAdmin_(params); const targetDate = String(params.date || Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "Asia/Seoul", "yyyy-MM-dd")).trim(); const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); const cacheKey = getAdminCacheKey_("classList", admin, targetDate); if (!isForceRefresh_(params)) { const cached = cache.get(cacheKey); if (cached) { return jsonOutput_(JSON.parse(cached)); } } const classes = []; const seen = {}; const dateInfo = getDateInfo_(targetDate); const attendanceSS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID); const videoLinkMap = getCourseClassVideoLinkMap_(); attendanceSS.getSheets().forEach(sheet => { const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (sheetName === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록)/.test(sheetName)) return; const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); if (!classBelongsToAdmin_(teacher, teacher, admin)) return; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 180); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 26); if (lastRow < 5 || lastCol < 2) return; const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getDisplayValues(); const blocks = buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_(values, sheetName, dateInfo); blocks.forEach(block => { const fullName = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, block.dayText, block.classText); if (!classBelongsToAdmin_(fullName, teacher, admin)) return; addClassItem_(classes, seen, fullName, teacher.replace(/T$/, ""), `출석부 ${sheetName}`, getCourseVideoLinkForClass_(fullName, videoLinkMap)); }); }); classes.sort((a, b) => String(a.className).localeCompare(String(b.className), "ko")); const payload = { status: "success", classes }; try { cache.put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(payload), 600); } catch (cacheErr) {} return jsonOutput_(payload); } catch (err) { return jsonOutput_({ status: "error", message: err.message }); } } function getActiveMonthColumnRangesForBlock_(values, blockStart, blockEnd, dateInfo) { if (!dateInfo || !dateInfo.valid) return []; const dateCols = []; const scanEnd = Math.min(blockEnd, blockStart + 6); // 요일/강사/반명/날짜 헤더 영역만 스캔 for (let r = blockStart; r <= scanEnd; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) { if (cellLooksLikeMonthDate_(row[c], dateInfo)) { dateCols.push(c); } } } if (dateCols.length === 0) return []; dateCols.sort((a, b) => a - b); const clusters = []; let start = dateCols[0]; let end = dateCols[0]; for (let i = 1; i < dateCols.length; i++) { const c = dateCols[i]; if (c <= end + 2) { end = c; } else { clusters.push({ start, end }); start = c; end = c; } } clusters.push({ start, end }); return clusters.map(group => ({ start: Math.max(0, group.start - 2), // NO/이름 열 포함 end: group.end + 1 // 비고 열 포함 })); } function columnInRanges_(col, ranges) { if (!ranges || ranges.length === 0) return true; return ranges.some(range => col >= range.start && col <= range.end); } function cellLooksLikeMonthDate_(value, dateInfo) { const text = String(value || "").replace(/\s/g, ""); if (!text) return false; const m = String(Number(dateInfo.mm)); const m2 = String(dateInfo.mm2); const slashDot = new RegExp(`(^|[^0-9])0?${m}[\\/.]\\d{1,2}([^0-9]|$)`); const korean = new RegExp(`(^|[^0-9])0?${m}월\\d{1,2}일?`); const slashDot2 = new RegExp(`(^|[^0-9])${m2}[\\/.]\\d{1,2}([^0-9]|$)`); return slashDot.test(text) || slashDot2.test(text) || korean.test(text); } function findNearestWeekdayText_(row, idx) { const weekdays = ["월요일", "화요일", "수요일", "목요일", "금요일", "토요일", "일요일"]; const candidates = []; for (let offset = 0; offset <= 4; offset++) { [idx - offset, idx + offset].forEach(i => { if (i < 0 || i >= row.length) return; const text = String(row[i] || "").trim(); if (weekdays.indexOf(text) !== -1) candidates.push(text); }); if (candidates.length) return candidates[0]; } return ""; } function findWeekdayAbove_(sheet, dayRowNo, idx, lastCol) { const weekdays = ["월요일", "화요일", "수요일", "목요일", "금요일", "토요일", "일요일"]; const startRow = Math.max(1, dayRowNo - 2); const numRows = dayRowNo - startRow + 1; const values = sheet.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, lastCol).getDisplayValues(); for (let r = values.length - 1; r >= 0; r--) { const text = findNearestWeekdayText_(values[r], idx); if (text && weekdays.indexOf(text) !== -1) return text; } return ""; } function findClassTextForBlock_(values, blockStart, headerRow, nameCol) { const start = Math.max(0, blockStart); const end = Math.max(start, headerRow - 1); // 1순위: 학생 이름 열 주변의 반명 셀 for (let r = end; r >= start; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; const found = findNearestClassTextInRow_(row, nameCol); if (found) return found; } // 2순위: 블록 상단 전체에서 반명처럼 보이는 가장 가까운 셀 let best = null; for (let r = end; r >= start; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) { const text = cleanClassCellText_(row[c]); if (!isAttendanceClassCellText_(text)) continue; const score = Math.abs(c - nameCol) + Math.abs(r - headerRow) * 2; if (!best || score < best.score) best = { text, score }; } } return best ? best.text : ""; } function formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, classText) { const text = String(classText || "").trim(); const day = String(dayText || "").trim(); const stripped = text.replace(/^\[[^\]]+T\]\s*/, "").trim(); return `[${teacher}]${day ? " - " + day : ""} ${stripped}`.replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim(); } function normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName) { const base = String(sheetName || "").replace(/^보관_?/, "").replace(/_?\d{4}.*$/, "").trim(); const m = base.match(/([가-힣]{2,4})T?/); if (m) return normalizeTeacherAlias_(m[1], true); return base || "강사"; } function cleanClassCellText_(value) { return String(value || "") .replace(/\r/g, "\n") .split("\n") .map(v => v.trim()) .filter(Boolean) .join(" ") .replace(/\s+/g, " ") .trim(); } function isAttendanceClassCellText_(text) { text = String(text || "").trim(); if (!text) return false; if (text.length < 3 || text.length > 80) return false; if (/^(NO|이름|출석현황|수업내용|비고|일요일|월요일|화요일|수요일|목요일|금요일|토요일)$/i.test(text)) return false; if (/^\d{1,2}([:~～-]|월|일|시)/.test(text)) return false; return /(반|초급|중급|기초|공채|더빙|스피치|연기|낭독|발음|리딩|애니메이션|입문|성인|청소년|초등)/.test(text); } function formatClassNameFromAttendance_(teacher, classText) { const text = String(classText || "").trim(); if (/^\[[^\]]+T\]/.test(text)) return text; return `[${teacher}] ${text}`; } function addClassItem_(classes, seen, className, teacher, source, videoLink) { className = String(className || "").trim(); if (!className) return; const key = normalizeForLooseMatch_(className); if (seen[key]) return; seen[key] = true; classes.push({ className, teacher: teacher || "", source: source || "", videoLink: String(videoLink || "").trim() }); } /** * 수강신청반목록 시트 D열을 반별 수업영상 링크로 사용합니다. * 구조: A열 사용여부 / B열 구분 / C열 반명 / D열 수업영상링크 */ function getCourseClassVideoLinkMap_() { const map = {}; try { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(COURSE_FORM_CLASSES_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return map; const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow(); const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 4); const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues(); values.forEach(function(row) { const useText = String(row[0] || "").trim().toLowerCase(); const isDisabled = /^(아니오|false|x|no|n|0|삭제|숨김|미사용)$/i.test(useText); if (isDisabled) return; const className = String(row[2] || "").trim(); const videoLink = String(row[3] || "").trim(); if (!className || !videoLink) return; const keys = getClassVideoLinkKeys_(className); keys.forEach(function(key) { if (key) map[key] = videoLink; }); }); } catch (err) {} return map; } function getCourseVideoLinkForClass_(className, map) { map = map || getCourseClassVideoLinkMap_(); const keys = getClassVideoLinkKeys_(className); for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) { if (keys[i] && map[keys[i]]) return map[keys[i]]; } return ""; } function getClassVideoLinkKeys_(className) { const raw = String(className || "").trim(); const noTeacher = raw.replace(/^\s*\[[^\]]+T?\]\s*[-–—]?\s*/g, "").trim(); const noBracketOnly = raw.replace(/\[[^\]]+T?\]/g, "").trim(); return [raw, noTeacher, noBracketOnly] .map(normalizeClassForVideoLink_) .filter(function(v, i, arr) { return v && arr.indexOf(v) === i; }); } function normalizeClassForVideoLink_(value) { return String(value || "") .replace(/김\s*인\s*혁/g, "김인형") .replace(/김\s*인\s*형/g, "김인형") .replace(/박\s*승\s*기/g, "박송") .replace(/박\s*송/g, "박송") .replace(/[\[\]\(\)]/g, "") .replace(/T/g, "") .replace(/[-–—]/g, "") .replace(/~/g, "～") .replace(/\s+/g, "") .trim() .normalize("NFC"); } function extractTeacherFromClass_(text) { text = String(text || ""); const m = text.match(/\[?([가-힣]{2,4})T\]?/); if (m) return normalizeTeacherAlias_(m[1], false); return ""; } function isClassLikeText_(text) { text = String(text || "").trim(); if (text.length < 4 || text.length > 80) return false; if (/^\d{1,2}(월|일|시)?$/.test(text)) return false; return /(T\]|T|반|초급|중급|기초|공채|더빙|스피치|연기|낭독|토요일|일요일|월요일|화요일|수요일|목요일|금요일)/.test(text); } function isAllClassQuery_(value) { const key = normalizeName(value || "").toLowerCase(); return key === "전체반" || key === "전체" || key === "all" || key === "allclasses"; } function getTeacherKeyFromClassQuery_(classQuery) { const teacher = extractTeacherFromClass_(classQuery || ""); return normalizeAdminTeacherKey_(teacher || ""); } function sheetCouldContainClassQuery_(sheetName, classQuery) { if (!classQuery || isAllClassQuery_(classQuery)) return true; const queryTeacherKey = getTeacherKeyFromClassQuery_(classQuery); if (!queryTeacherKey) return true; const sheetTeacherKey = normalizeAdminTeacherKey_(normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName)); if (!sheetTeacherKey) return true; return sheetTeacherKey.indexOf(queryTeacherKey) !== -1 || queryTeacherKey.indexOf(sheetTeacherKey) !== -1; } function adminGetAttendanceSnapshot_(params) { try { const admin = requireAdmin_(params); const date = String(params.date || "").trim(); let classQuery = String(params.className || "").trim(); if (isAllClassQuery_(classQuery)) classQuery = ""; const keyword = String(params.keyword || "").trim(); const statusFilter = String(params.statusFilter || "").trim(); if (!date) throw new Error("수업일이 필요합니다."); const students = getStudentsForAdmin_(); let records = scanAttendanceSheets_(date, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter, students) .filter(function(record) { return attendanceRecordBelongsToAdmin_(record, admin); }) .map(function(record) { return sanitizeAttendanceRecordForRole_(attachClassroomToAttendanceRecord_(record), admin); }); // 반명을 선택했는데 0건이면 예전에는 같은 날짜 전체 시트를 다시 훑었습니다. // 이 과정이 5~10초 이상 걸릴 수 있어 제거하고, 선택 반 블록 직접 탐색 fallback만 실행합니다. // 성인 토요 A/B반처럼 반명은 목록에 뜨지만 학생 행을 못 읽는 블록을 위해, // 선택한 반명 셀을 먼저 찾고 그 아래의 '이름' 헤더를 기준으로 학생을 직접 읽는 보정 로직입니다. if (records.length === 0 && classQuery) { records = scanAttendanceSheetsBySelectedClassBlockFallback_(date, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter, students, admin) .map(function(record) { return sanitizeAttendanceRecordForRole_(attachClassroomToAttendanceRecord_(record), admin); }); } return jsonOutput_({ status: "success", admin, records, count: records.length, message: `출석부에서 ${records.length}건을 반영했습니다.` }); } catch (err) { return jsonOutput_({ status: "error", message: err.message }); } } function scanAttendanceSheets_(date, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter, students) { const attendanceSS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID); const studentMap = {}; students.forEach(s => studentMap[s.nameKey] = s); const records = []; const seen = {}; const dateInfo = getDateInfo_(date); attendanceSS.getSheets().forEach(sheet => { const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (sheetName === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록)/.test(sheetName)) return; if (!sheetCouldContainClassQuery_(sheetName, classQuery)) return; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 180); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 26); if (lastRow < 5 || lastCol < 2) return; const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol); const values = range.getDisplayValues(); const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); let blocks = buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_(values, sheetName, dateInfo); // 특정 반을 선택한 경우, 선택 반과 관련 없는 블록은 배경색을 읽기 전에 제외합니다. // getBackgrounds()가 가장 무거운 호출 중 하나라서 체감 속도에 큰 영향을 줍니다. if (classQuery) { blocks = blocks.filter(function(block) { const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, block.dayText, block.classText); const instructor = teacher.replace(/T$/, ""); return attendanceClassQueryMatchesRecord_(classQuery, { className: className, instructor: instructor }); }); } if (!blocks.length) return; const backgrounds = range.getBackgrounds(); blocks.forEach(block => { const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, block.dayText, block.classText); const instructor = teacher.replace(/T$/, ""); const panel = block.panel; for (let r = block.headerRow + 1; r <= block.blockEnd && r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const bgRow = backgrounds[r] || []; const noText = String(row[panel.noCol] || "").trim(); const nameText = String(row[panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); const raw = String(row[block.dateCol] || "").trim(); const rawStatus = normalizeAttendanceStatus_(raw); const nameSpecial = getSpecialStatusByColor_(bgRow[panel.nameCol]); const dateSpecial = getSpecialStatusByColor_(bgRow[block.dateCol]); const specialStatus = dateSpecial || nameSpecial || ""; const memo = getPanelMemo_(row, panel); // 1) 일반 재원생: 이름 열(C/K 등)에 학생명이 있음 if (isNameCellLikeStudent_(nameText)) { const nameKey = normalizeName(nameText); const student = studentMap[nameKey] || makeFallbackStudent_(nameText, instructor); const status = rawStatus || "미체크"; const record = makeAttendanceRecord_(date, student, instructor, className, status, specialStatus, memo); addAttendanceRecordIfMatches_(seen, record, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter); } // 2) 보강생: 해당 날짜 칸(D~G/L~O 등)에 학생명이 직접 적혀 있음 const rawNameKey = normalizeName(raw); const rawLooksLikeStudentName = rawNameKey && !rawStatus && /^[가-힣]{2,5}$/.test(rawNameKey); if (rawLooksLikeStudentName) { const student = studentMap[rawNameKey] || makeFallbackStudent_(raw, instructor); const status = dateSpecial || "미체크"; const record = makeAttendanceRecord_(date, student, instructor, className, status, dateSpecial || specialStatus, memo); addAttendanceRecordIfMatches_(seen, record, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter); } } }); }); Object.keys(seen).forEach(k => records.push(seen[k])); records.sort((a, b) => [a.instructor, a.className, a.studentName].join("|").localeCompare([b.instructor, b.className, b.studentName].join("|"), "ko")); return records; } /** * 선택한 반명은 찾았지만 학생 목록이 0건으로 나오는 일부 성인 토요 A/B반 보정용. * 반명 셀을 먼저 찾고, 그 아래쪽에서 "이름" 헤더를 찾은 뒤 그 아래 학생명 행을 읽습니다. * 기존 buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_가 놓치는 병합/블록 변형 구조를 보완합니다. */ function scanAttendanceSheetsBySelectedClassBlockFallback_(date, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter, students, admin) { const attendanceSS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID); const studentMap = {}; students.forEach(function(s) { studentMap[s.nameKey] = s; }); const records = []; const seen = {}; const dateInfo = getDateInfo_(date); if (!dateInfo || !dateInfo.valid || !classQuery) return records; attendanceSS.getSheets().forEach(function(sheet) { const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (sheetName === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록)/.test(sheetName)) return; if (!sheetCouldContainClassQuery_(sheetName, classQuery)) return; const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); if (!classBelongsToAdmin_(classQuery, teacher, admin)) return; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 180); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 26); if (lastRow < 5 || lastCol < 2) return; const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol); const values = range.getDisplayValues(); const backgrounds = range.getBackgrounds(); const panels = getAttendanceMonthPanelsForDate_(values, dateInfo); panels.forEach(function(panel) { const classCells = findMatchingClassCellsInPanel_(values, panel, teacher, classQuery); classCells.forEach(function(classCell) { const nameHeader = findNameHeaderBelowClassCell_(values, classCell.row, panel); if (!nameHeader) return; const dateCol = findDateColumnInAttendancePanel_(values, nameHeader.row, panel, dateInfo); if (dateCol < 0) return; const classText = classCell.classText || findClassTextInAttendancePanel_(values, nameHeader.row, panel); if (!classText) return; const dayText = findDayTextInAttendancePanel_(values, nameHeader.row, panel); const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, classText); const instructor = teacher.replace(/T$/, ""); if (!attendanceClassQueryMatchesRecord_(classQuery, { className: className, instructor: instructor })) { return; } // 다음 반 블록 전까지만 읽습니다. 일반적으로 8명 정원이지만, 여유를 두고 최대 12행까지 허용합니다. const endRow = findStudentBlockEndAfterHeader_(values, nameHeader.row, panel); for (let r = nameHeader.row + 1; r <= endRow && r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const bgRow = backgrounds[r] || []; const nameText = String(row[nameHeader.col] || "").trim(); const raw = String(row[dateCol] || "").trim(); const rawStatus = normalizeAttendanceStatus_(raw); const nameSpecial = getSpecialStatusByColor_(bgRow[nameHeader.col]); const dateSpecial = getSpecialStatusByColor_(bgRow[dateCol]); const specialStatus = dateSpecial || nameSpecial || ""; const memo = getPanelMemo_(row, panel); if (isNameCellLikeStudent_(nameText)) { const nameKey = normalizeName(nameText); const student = studentMap[nameKey] || makeFallbackStudent_(nameText, instructor); const status = rawStatus || "미체크"; const record = makeAttendanceRecord_(date, student, instructor, className, status, specialStatus, memo); addAttendanceRecordIfMatches_(seen, record, "", keyword, statusFilter); } // 날짜 칸에 보강생 이름이 직접 적힌 경우 const rawNameKey = normalizeName(raw); const rawLooksLikeStudentName = rawNameKey && !rawStatus && /^[가-힣]{2,5}$/.test(rawNameKey); if (rawLooksLikeStudentName) { const student = studentMap[rawNameKey] || makeFallbackStudent_(raw, instructor); const status = dateSpecial || "미체크"; const record = makeAttendanceRecord_(date, student, instructor, className, status, dateSpecial || specialStatus, memo); addAttendanceRecordIfMatches_(seen, record, "", keyword, statusFilter); } } }); }); }); Object.keys(seen).forEach(function(k) { records.push(seen[k]); }); records.sort(function(a, b) { return [a.instructor, a.className, a.studentName].join("|") .localeCompare([b.instructor, b.className, b.studentName].join("|"), "ko"); }); return records; } function findMatchingClassCellsInPanel_(values, panel, teacher, classQuery) { const found = []; const query = String(classQuery || "").trim(); if (!query) return found; for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = cleanClassCellText_(row[c]); if (!isAttendanceClassCellText_(text)) continue; const dayText = findDayTextAroundClassCell_(values, r, panel); const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, text); const instructor = teacher.replace(/T$/, ""); if (attendanceClassQueryMatchesRecord_(query, { className: className, instructor: instructor })) { found.push({ row: r, col: c, classText: text, className: className }); } } } return found; } function findDayTextAroundClassCell_(values, classRow, panel) { const weekdays = ["월요일", "화요일", "수요일", "목요일", "금요일", "토요일", "일요일"]; const startRow = Math.max(0, classRow - 4); const endRow = Math.min(values.length - 1, classRow + 1); for (let r = classRow; r >= startRow; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").trim(); if (weekdays.indexOf(text) !== -1) return text; } } for (let r = classRow + 1; r <= endRow; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").trim(); if (weekdays.indexOf(text) !== -1) return text; } } return ""; } function findNameHeaderBelowClassCell_(values, classRow, panel) { const maxRow = Math.min(values.length - 1, classRow + 6); // 1순위: 패널의 기본 이름 열(C/K) for (let r = classRow; r <= maxRow; r++) { const text = String((values[r] || [])[panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); if (text === "이름" || text === "학생명") { return { row: r, col: panel.nameCol }; } } // 2순위: 패널 안 전체에서 이름 헤더 탐색 for (let r = classRow; r <= maxRow; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").trim(); if (text === "이름" || text === "학생명") { return { row: r, col: c }; } } } return null; } function findStudentBlockEndAfterHeader_(values, headerRow, panel) { const hardLimit = Math.min(values.length - 1, headerRow + 12); let lastUsefulRow = headerRow; for (let r = headerRow + 1; r <= hardLimit; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const noText = String(row[panel.noCol] || "").trim(); const nameText = String(row[panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); // 다음 블록 헤더 또는 구분 행 감지 const rowText = row.slice(panel.start, panel.end + 1).join(" ").trim(); if (r > headerRow + 1 && /(출석현황|수업내용|요일|월요일|화요일|수요일|목요일|금요일|토요일|일요일)/.test(rowText)) { break; } if (noText || nameText) { lastUsefulRow = r; continue; } // 완전 빈 행이 나오면 한 줄 정도는 여유를 주고, 이후는 중단 const hasAny = row.slice(panel.start, panel.end + 1).some(function(v) { return String(v || "").trim(); }); if (!hasAny && r > lastUsefulRow + 1) break; } return Math.max(lastUsefulRow, Math.min(hardLimit, headerRow + 8)); } function getDateInfo_(date) { const d = new Date(date + "T00:00:00"); if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return { valid: false, patterns: [] }; const yyyy = String(d.getFullYear()); const mm = String(d.getMonth() + 1); const dd = String(d.getDate()); const mm2 = mm.padStart(2, "0"); const dd2 = dd.padStart(2, "0"); const weekday = getKoreanWeekday_(d); // v93 중요: // 출석부에서는 "1주차 06/06"처럼 날짜가 주차 문구와 함께 적혀 있습니다. // 따라서 오늘 날짜는 반드시 06/01, 6/1, 6월1일처럼 "월+일"이 함께 있는 형태만 인정합니다. // 숫자 1 단독, 1주차, 1일 단독은 날짜로 인정하지 않습니다. return { valid: true, yyyy, mm, dd, mm2, dd2, weekday, patterns: [ `${yyyy}-${mm2}-${dd2}`, `${yyyy}.${mm2}.${dd2}`, `${yyyy}/${mm2}/${dd2}`, `${mm}/${dd}`, `${mm2}/${dd2}`, `${mm}.${dd}`, `${mm2}.${dd2}`, `${mm}월${dd}일`, `${mm2}월${dd2}일` ] }; } function findAttendanceBlocks_(values, sheetName) { // v17 이후 실제 출석부 조회는 buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_를 사용합니다. // 기존 호출부 호환을 위해 현재 날짜 기준으로 래핑합니다. const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "Asia/Seoul", "yyyy-MM-dd"); return buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_(values, sheetName, getDateInfo_(today)); } function findDateColumnInHeaderRows_(values, headerRow, blockStart, blockEnd, dateInfo, nameCol) { if (!dateInfo || !dateInfo.valid) return -1; const startRow = Math.max(blockStart, headerRow - 2); const endRow = Math.min(blockEnd, headerRow + 1); // 이름 열 오른쪽의 날짜 칸을 우선 탐색합니다. for (let r = endRow; r >= startRow; r--) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = nameCol + 1; c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!text) continue; if (dateInfo.patterns.indexOf(text) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "/" + dateInfo.dd) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm2 + "/" + dateInfo.dd2) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "." + dateInfo.dd) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm2 + "." + dateInfo.dd2) !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "월" + dateInfo.dd + "일") !== -1) return c; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm2 + "월" + dateInfo.dd2 + "일") !== -1) return c; } } return -1; } function makeFallbackStudent_(name, instructor) { return { studentNo: "", name: String(name || "").trim(), nameKey: normalizeName(name), studentPhone: "", parentPhone: "", className: "", memo: "", instructor: normalizeTeacherAlias_(instructor || "", false) }; } function attachClassroomToAttendanceRecord_(record) { const out = Object.assign({}, record || {}); out.classroom = resolveAttendanceClassroom_( out.date, out.className, out.instructor, out.classroom || out.roomName || out.room || "" ); return out; } function resolveAttendanceClassroom_(date, className, instructor, directRoom) { const direct = String(directRoom || "").trim(); if (direct) return direct; const classText = String(className || "").trim(); if (!classText) return ""; const targetDate = String(date || Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "Asia/Seoul", "yyyy-MM-dd")).trim(); const weekday = extractWeekdayFromText_(classText) || getKoreanWeekdayFromDateString_(targetDate); const teacher = String(instructor || "").trim() || extractTeacherFromClass_(classText) || (typeof extractTeacherFromTabletClassName_ === "function" ? extractTeacherFromTabletClassName_(classText) : ""); return safeFindRoomForAttendanceClass_(targetDate, weekday, teacher, classText); } function safeFindRoomForAttendanceClass_(date, weekday, instructor, className) { try { if (typeof findRoomForClassFast_ === "function") { return String(findRoomForClassFast_(date, weekday, instructor, className) || "").trim(); } } catch (err) { // 강의실 조회 실패 시 문자 발송 자체가 막히면 안 되므로 빈값으로 처리합니다. } return ""; } function getKoreanWeekdayFromDateString_(dateText) { const text = String(dateText || "").trim(); const m = text.match(/^(\d{4})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})$/); if (!m) return ""; const d = new Date(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3])); if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return ""; return ["일요일", "월요일", "화요일", "수요일", "목요일", "금요일", "토요일"][d.getDay()] || ""; } function makeAttendanceRecord_(date, student, instructor, className, status, specialStatus, memo) { return { date, studentName: student.name || "", studentNo: student.studentNo || "", studentPhone: student.studentPhone || "", parentPhone: student.parentPhone || "", instructor: normalizeTeacherAlias_(student.instructor || instructor || extractTeacherFromClass_(className), false), className: className || student.className || "", classroom: resolveAttendanceClassroom_(date, className || student.className || "", student.instructor || instructor || ""), status: status || "미체크", specialStatus: specialStatus || "", memo: memo || "" }; } function addAttendanceRecordIfMatches_(seen, record, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter) { if (!record || !record.studentName) return; if (!attendanceRecordMatches_(record, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter)) return; const key = [record.date, record.studentName, normalizeForLooseMatch_(record.className), record.specialStatus || record.status].join("|"); if (!seen[key] || seen[key].status === "미체크") seen[key] = record; } function findStatusForStudentRow_(values, backgrounds, r, nameCol, date) { const dateCol = findDateColumnNear_(values, r, date); if (dateCol >= 0 && dateCol !== nameCol) { const raw = String(values[r][dateCol] || "").trim(); return { status: normalizeAttendanceStatus_(raw), raw, col: columnToLetter_(dateCol + 1), colIndex: dateCol }; } const start = Math.max(0, nameCol - 2); const end = Math.min(values[r].length - 1, nameCol + 12); for (let c = start; c <= end; c++) { if (c === nameCol) continue; const raw = String(values[r][c] || "").trim(); const status = normalizeAttendanceStatus_(raw); if (status && status !== "미체크") return { status, raw, col: columnToLetter_(c + 1), colIndex: c }; } return { status: "미체크", raw: "", col: "", colIndex: -1 }; } function findDateColumnNear_(values, r, date) { const d = new Date(date + "T00:00:00"); if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return -1; const yyyy = String(d.getFullYear()); const mm = String(d.getMonth() + 1); const dd = String(d.getDate()); const mm2 = mm.padStart(2, "0"); const dd2 = dd.padStart(2, "0"); const patterns = [ `${yyyy}-${mm2}-${dd2}`, `${mm}/${dd}`, `${mm2}/${dd2}`, `${mm}.${dd}`, `${mm2}.${dd2}`, `${mm}월${dd}일`, `${dd}`, `${dd}일` ]; const startRow = Math.max(0, r - 10); const endRow = Math.min(values.length - 1, r); for (let rr = endRow; rr >= startRow; rr--) { for (let c = 0; c < values[rr].length; c++) { const text = String(values[rr][c] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!text) continue; if (patterns.indexOf(text) !== -1) return c; if (text === dd && c > 0) return c; } } return -1; } function findSpecialStatusForStudentRow_(backgrounds, r, nameCol, statusCol) { const candidates = []; if (backgrounds && backgrounds[r]) { candidates.push(backgrounds[r][nameCol]); if (statusCol !== undefined && statusCol >= 0) candidates.push(backgrounds[r][statusCol]); } for (let i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) { const status = getSpecialStatusByColor_(candidates[i]); if (status) return status; } return ""; } function getSpecialStatusByColor_(bgColor) { const color = String(bgColor || "").toLowerCase().trim(); if (!color || color === "#ffffff" || color === "white") return ""; const exactMap = { "#ffff00": "신규", "#fff2cc": "신규", "#fce5cd": "신규", "#ffd966": "신규", "#ffe599": "신규", "#b4a7d6": "반이동", "#d9d2e9": "반이동", "#c9daf8": "반이동", "#c27ba0": "반이동", "#eadcf8": "반이동", "#d5a6bd": "반이동", "#92d050": "보강", "#b6d7a8": "보강", "#d9ead3": "보강", "#a9d18e": "보강", "#00ff00": "보강", "#b7e1cd": "보강" }; if (exactMap[color]) return exactMap[color]; const rgb = hexToRgb_(color); if (!rgb) return ""; const r = rgb.r, g = rgb.g, b = rgb.b; // 노란색 계열: R/G 높고 B 낮음 if (r >= 220 && g >= 190 && b <= 150) return "신규"; // 초록색 계열: G가 높고 R/B보다 확실히 큼 if (g >= 150 && g >= r + 25 && g >= b + 25) return "보강"; // 보라색 계열: R/B가 높고 G가 낮거나 중간 if (b >= 140 && r >= 120 && g <= 190 && Math.abs(r - b) <= 90) return "반이동"; return ""; } function hexToRgb_(hex) { const m = String(hex || "").match(/^#?([0-9a-f]{6})$/i); if (!m) return null; const n = parseInt(m[1], 16); return { r: (n >> 16) & 255, g: (n >> 8) & 255, b: n & 255 }; } function normalizeAttendanceStatus_(raw) { const text = String(raw || "").replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase(); if (!text) return "미체크"; if (["O", "○", "ㅇ", "출", "출석", "TRUE", "V", "✓", "✔"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "출석"; if (["X", "×", "✕", "결", "결석", "FALSE"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "결석"; if (["지", "지각", "△", "늦음"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "지각"; if (["보", "보강"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "보강"; if (["휴", "휴원"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "휴원"; if (["신", "신규"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "신규"; if (["이", "반이동", "이동"].indexOf(text) !== -1) return "반이동"; return ""; } function inferClassName_(values, r, c, sheetName, classQuery, student) { const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); const dayRows = [2, 16, 30, 44, 58, 72, 86, 100]; // 실제 시트 3행부터 14행 간격, 0-based let blockDayRow = -1; for (let i = 0; i < dayRows.length; i++) { if (dayRows[i] <= r) blockDayRow = dayRows[i]; } if (blockDayRow >= 0 && values[blockDayRow]) { const dayText = findNearestWeekdayText_(values[blockDayRow], c); const classRowIndexes = [blockDayRow + 2, blockDayRow + 3]; for (let k = 0; k < classRowIndexes.length; k++) { const rr = classRowIndexes[k]; if (!values[rr]) continue; const classText = findNearestClassTextInRow_(values[rr], c); if (classText) return formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, classText); } } const candidates = []; for (let rr = Math.max(0, r - 8); rr <= r; rr++) { if (!values[rr]) continue; values[rr].forEach(v => { const text = String(v || "").trim(); if (isClassLikeText_(text)) candidates.push(text); }); } if (student.className) candidates.push(student.className); if (sheetName) candidates.push(sheetName); candidates.sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length); let picked = candidates[0] || sheetName || ""; if (picked && !/^\[[^\]]+T\]/.test(picked)) { if (teacher && isAttendanceClassCellText_(picked)) picked = formatClassNameFromAttendance_(teacher, picked); } return picked; } function findNearestClassTextInRow_(row, idx) { const candidates = []; for (let offset = 0; offset <= 8; offset++) { [idx - offset, idx + offset].forEach(i => { if (i < 0 || i >= row.length) return; const text = cleanClassCellText_(row[i]); if (isAttendanceClassCellText_(text)) candidates.push({ text, offset }); }); if (candidates.length) return candidates[0].text; } return ""; } function findMemoForStudentRow_(values, r) { if (!values || !values[r]) return ""; // 요청 기준: 출석부 H열 비고만 메모로 사용합니다. 비어 있으면 메모도 빈칸입니다. return String(values[r][7] || "").trim(); } function attendanceRecordMatches_(record, classQuery, keyword, statusFilter) { // 반명은 출석부 병합셀/공백/하이픈/시간 표기 차이 때문에 단순 includes로만 보면 누락됩니다. // 따라서 교사명 + 요일 + 핵심 반명 기준으로 한 번 더 느슨하게 비교합니다. if (classQuery && !isAllClassQuery_(classQuery) && !attendanceClassQueryMatchesRecord_(classQuery, record)) return false; // 학생명 검색 전용: 강사명/반명/전화번호는 검색 대상에서 제외합니다. if (keyword) { const studentName = String((record && record.studentName) || "").toLowerCase(); if (studentName.indexOf(String(keyword).toLowerCase()) === -1) return false; } if (statusFilter && record.status !== statusFilter && record.specialStatus !== statusFilter) return false; return true; } function attendanceClassQueryMatchesRecord_(classQuery, record) { const query = String(classQuery || "").trim(); if (!query || isAllClassQuery_(query)) return true; const recordClass = String((record && record.className) || "").trim(); const recordInstructor = String((record && record.instructor) || "").trim(); const blob = [recordClass, recordInstructor].join(" "); const qLoose = normalizeForLooseMatch_(query).toLowerCase(); const bLoose = normalizeForLooseMatch_(blob).toLowerCase(); if (bLoose.indexOf(qLoose) !== -1 || qLoose.indexOf(bLoose) !== -1) return true; const qTeacher = normalizeAdminTeacherKey_(extractTeacherFromClass_(query) || query); const bTeacher = normalizeAdminTeacherKey_(extractTeacherFromClass_(recordClass) || recordInstructor); const teacherOk = !qTeacher || !bTeacher || bTeacher.indexOf(qTeacher) !== -1 || qTeacher.indexOf(bTeacher) !== -1; if (!teacherOk) return false; const qDay = extractWeekdayFromText_(query); const bDay = extractWeekdayFromText_(recordClass); const dayOk = !qDay || !bDay || qDay === bDay; if (!dayOk) return false; const qCore = normalizeClassCoreForCompare_(query); const bCore = normalizeClassCoreForCompare_(recordClass); if (!qCore || !bCore) return true; return bCore.indexOf(qCore) !== -1 || qCore.indexOf(bCore) !== -1; } function extractWeekdayFromText_(value) { const text = String(value || ""); const days = ["월요일", "화요일", "수요일", "목요일", "금요일", "토요일", "일요일"]; for (let i = 0; i < days.length; i++) { if (text.indexOf(days[i]) !== -1) return days[i]; } return ""; } function normalizeClassCoreForCompare_(value) { return String(value || "") .replace(/\[[^\]]+\]/g, "") .replace(/[가-힣]{2,4}T/g, "") .replace(/월요일|화요일|수요일|목요일|금요일|토요일|일요일/g, "") .replace(/\d{1,2}\s*[:：]\s*\d{2}\s*[~～\-]\s*\d{1,2}\s*[:：]\s*\d{2}/g, "") .replace(/\d{1,2}\s*[:：]\s*\d{2}/g, "") .replace(/[()（）\[\]\-~～:：\s]/g, "") .replace(/A반/g, "A") .replace(/B반/g, "B") .replace(/C반/g, "C") .trim() .normalize("NFC") .toLowerCase(); } function columnToLetter_(col) { let temp = ""; while (col > 0) { const rem = (col - 1) % 26; temp = String.fromCharCode(65 + rem) + temp; col = Math.floor((col - rem) / 26); } return temp; } function adminSaveAttendance_(params) { try { const admin = requireAdmin_(params); const records = parseJsonParam_(params.records, []); if (!records.length) throw new Error("저장할 출석 기록이 없습니다."); const writeResult = writeAdminAttendanceRecordsToBook_(records, admin); // 감사 로그는 기존 웹출석기록 시트에 계속 남깁니다. const logRecords = (writeResult.results || []).map(function(result) { const r = Object.assign({}, result.record || {}); r.status = result.normalizedStatus || r.status || ""; r.memo = String(r.memo || "").trim(); if (!result.ok) { r.memo = (r.memo ? r.memo + " / " : "") + "출석부반영:" + (result.message || "실패"); } return r; }); appendWebAttendanceRecords_(logRecords.length ? logRecords : records, admin); const message = "출석부 즉시 반영 완료: " + writeResult.updated + "건" + (writeResult.skipped ? " / 보호·건너뜀 " + writeResult.skipped + "건" : "") + (writeResult.failed ? " / 실패 " + writeResult.failed + "건" : ""); return jsonOutput_({ status: "success", count: records.length, updated: writeResult.updated, skipped: writeResult.skipped, failed: writeResult.failed, results: writeResult.results, message: message }); } catch (err) { return jsonOutput_({ status: "error", message: err.message }); } } function writeAdminAttendanceRecordsToBook_(records, admin) { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) { throw new Error("다른 출석부 작업이 진행 중입니다. 잠시 후 다시 시도해주세요."); } try { const attendanceSS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID); const results = []; let updated = 0; let skipped = 0; let failed = 0; records.forEach(function(record) { const result = writeOneAdminAttendanceRecordToBook_(attendanceSS, record, admin); results.push(result); if (result.ok) updated++; else if (result.skipped) skipped++; else failed++; }); SpreadsheetApp.flush(); return { updated: updated, skipped: skipped, failed: failed, results: results }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function writeOneAdminAttendanceRecordToBook_(attendanceSS, record, admin) { const r = Object.assign({}, record || {}); const studentName = String(r.studentName || r.name || "").trim(); const date = String(r.date || r.classDate || "").trim(); const normalizedStatus = normalizeAdminAttendanceStatusForWrite_(r.status || r.attendanceStatus || r.value || ""); const cellValue = adminAttendanceCellValueForStatus_(normalizedStatus); if (!studentName) { return { ok: false, skipped: false, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, message: "학생명이 없습니다." }; } if (!date) { return { ok: false, skipped: false, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, message: "수업일이 없습니다." }; } const target = findAdminAttendanceTargetCell_(attendanceSS, r, admin); if (!target) { return { ok: false, skipped: false, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, message: "출석부에서 대상 학생/날짜 칸을 찾지 못했습니다." }; } if (target.skipped) { return { ok: false, skipped: true, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, sheetName: target.sheetName || "", cellA1: target.cellA1 || "", message: target.message || "보호 대상 칸이어서 건너뜀" }; } if (!adminCanWriteAttendanceRecord_(admin, { studentName: studentName, className: target.className || r.className || "", instructor: target.instructor || r.instructor || "" })) { return { ok: false, skipped: false, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, sheetName: target.sheet ? target.sheet.getName() : "", cellA1: target.cellA1 || "", message: "해당 반/강사의 출석부를 수정할 권한이 없습니다." }; } const range = target.sheet.getRange(target.row, target.col); const currentText = String(range.getDisplayValue() || "").trim(); // 보강생처럼 날짜칸에 학생명이 직접 적혀 있는 경우 이름을 O/X로 덮어쓰면 안 됩니다. if (adminCellLooksLikeStudentNameForWrite_(currentText)) { return { ok: false, skipped: true, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, sheetName: target.sheet.getName(), cellA1: range.getA1Notation(), message: "날짜칸에 학생명이 직접 적혀 있어 보호 처리했습니다." }; } if (cellValue === "") { range.clearContent(); } else { range.setValue(cellValue); } return { ok: true, skipped: false, record: r, normalizedStatus: normalizedStatus, writtenValue: cellValue, sheetName: target.sheet.getName(), cellA1: range.getA1Notation(), className: target.className || r.className || "", instructor: target.instructor || r.instructor || "", message: "반영 완료" }; } function normalizeAdminAttendanceStatusForWrite_(value) { const raw = String(value || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!raw || raw === "-" || raw === "미체크" || raw === "미출결" || raw === "clear" || raw === "CLEAR") { return "미체크"; } if (/^(O|o|○|ㅇ|출|출석|참석|등원)$/.test(raw)) return "출석"; if (/^(X|x|×|✕|결|결석|미등원)$/.test(raw)) return "결석"; if (raw.indexOf("지각") !== -1 || raw === "△") return "지각"; if (raw.indexOf("휴원") !== -1) return "휴원"; if (raw.indexOf("보강") !== -1) return "보강"; if (raw.indexOf("신규") !== -1 || raw.indexOf("첫수업") !== -1) return "신규"; if (raw.indexOf("반이동") !== -1 || raw.indexOf("반변경") !== -1) return "반이동"; return raw; } function adminAttendanceCellValueForStatus_(status) { const normalized = normalizeAdminAttendanceStatusForWrite_(status); if (normalized === "출석") return "O"; if (normalized === "결석") return "X"; if (normalized === "미체크") return ""; return normalized; } function adminCellLooksLikeStudentNameForWrite_(value) { const text = String(value || "").trim(); if (!text) return false; let normalizedStatus = ""; try { if (typeof normalizeAttendanceStatus_ === "function") { normalizedStatus = normalizeAttendanceStatus_(text); } } catch (ignore) {} if (!normalizedStatus) { normalizedStatus = normalizeAdminAttendanceStatusForWrite_(text); if (["출석", "결석", "지각", "휴원", "보강", "신규", "반이동", "미체크"].indexOf(normalizedStatus) !== -1) { return false; } } const nameKey = normalizeName(text); return /^[가-힣]{2,5}$/.test(nameKey); } function findAdminAttendanceTargetCell_(attendanceSS, record, admin) { const date = String(record.date || record.classDate || "").trim(); const studentNameKey = normalizeName(record.studentName || record.name || ""); if (!date || !studentNameKey) return null; const dateInfo = adminBuildDateInfoForAttendanceWrite_(date); if (!dateInfo) return null; const sheets = attendanceSS.getSheets(); for (let s = 0; s < sheets.length; s++) { const sheet = sheets[s]; const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (adminShouldSkipAttendanceWriteSheet_(sheetName)) continue; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 220); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 80); if (lastRow < 3 || lastCol < 3) continue; const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getDisplayValues(); const blockTarget = findAdminAttendanceTargetByExistingBlocks_(sheet, values, dateInfo, record, admin); if (blockTarget) return blockTarget; const genericTarget = findAdminAttendanceTargetByGenericScan_(sheet, values, dateInfo, record, admin); if (genericTarget) return genericTarget; } return null; } function adminShouldSkipAttendanceWriteSheet_(sheetName) { const name = String(sheetName || "").trim(); if (typeof WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME !== "undefined" && name === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return true; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록|예약|문자|로그|태블릿|관리자)/.test(name)) return true; return false; } function findAdminAttendanceTargetByExistingBlocks_(sheet, values, dateInfo, record, admin) { if (typeof buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_ !== "function") return null; let blocks = []; try { blocks = buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_(values, sheet.getName(), dateInfo) || []; } catch (err1) { try { blocks = buildAttendanceBlocksForDate_(values, dateInfo, sheet.getName()) || []; } catch (err2) { blocks = []; } } if (!blocks || !blocks.length) return null; const targetNameKey = normalizeName(record.studentName || record.name || ""); for (let i = 0; i < blocks.length; i++) { const block = blocks[i] || {}; const panel = block.panel || {}; const nameCol = Number(panel.nameCol); const dateCol = Number(block.dateCol); const startRow = Number(panel.startRow); const endRow = Number(panel.endRow); if (!Number.isFinite(nameCol) || !Number.isFinite(dateCol) || !Number.isFinite(startRow) || !Number.isFinite(endRow)) { continue; } const instructor = block.instructor || adminInferInstructorFromSheetName_(sheet.getName()); const className = block.className || record.className || ""; if (!adminAttendanceTargetScopeMatches_(record, className, instructor, sheet.getName())) continue; for (let r = Math.max(0, startRow); r <= Math.min(values.length - 1, endRow); r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const nameText = String(row[nameCol] || "").trim(); const dateText = String(row[dateCol] || "").trim(); // 일반 재원생: 이름 열의 학생명과 매칭되면 같은 행의 날짜칸에 기록합니다. if (normalizeName(nameText) === targetNameKey) { return { sheet: sheet, row: r + 1, col: dateCol + 1, className: className, instructor: instructor, cellA1: adminColumnToLetter_(dateCol + 1) + (r + 1) }; } // 보강생: 날짜칸에 학생명이 직접 들어간 구조는 보호합니다. if (normalizeName(dateText) === targetNameKey && adminCellLooksLikeStudentNameForWrite_(dateText)) { return { skipped: true, sheetName: sheet.getName(), cellA1: adminColumnToLetter_(dateCol + 1) + (r + 1), className: className, instructor: instructor, message: "보강생 이름이 날짜칸에 직접 입력된 구조라 O/X로 덮어쓰지 않았습니다." }; } } } return null; } function findAdminAttendanceTargetByGenericScan_(sheet, values, dateInfo, record, admin) { const targetNameKey = normalizeName(record.studentName || record.name || ""); if (!targetNameKey) return null; const sheetInstructor = adminInferInstructorFromSheetName_(sheet.getName()); if (!adminAttendanceTargetScopeMatches_(record, record.className || "", sheetInstructor, sheet.getName(), true)) { return null; } for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) { const cellText = String(row[c] || "").trim(); if (normalizeName(cellText) !== targetNameKey) continue; // 날짜칸에 학생명이 직접 있는 경우는 보강생 가능성이 높으므로 보호 if (adminColumnHasTargetDateHeader_(values, c, r, dateInfo)) { return { skipped: true, sheetName: sheet.getName(), cellA1: adminColumnToLetter_(c + 1) + (r + 1), className: record.className || "", instructor: record.instructor || sheetInstructor, message: "날짜칸에 학생명이 직접 입력된 구조라 O/X로 덮어쓰지 않았습니다." }; } const dateCol = adminFindDateColumnForStudentRow_(values, r, c, dateInfo); if (dateCol < 0) continue; return { sheet: sheet, row: r + 1, col: dateCol + 1, className: record.className || "", instructor: record.instructor || sheetInstructor, cellA1: adminColumnToLetter_(dateCol + 1) + (r + 1) }; } } return null; } function adminFindDateColumnForStudentRow_(values, rowIndex, nameCol, dateInfo) { const maxCol = values[0] ? values[0].length : 0; // 이름 열 오른쪽 날짜칸을 우선 탐색합니다. for (let offset = 1; offset <= 8; offset++) { const c = nameCol + offset; if (c >= maxCol) break; if (adminColumnHasTargetDateHeader_(values, c, rowIndex, dateInfo)) return c; } // 일부 표 변형을 대비해 주변 열도 보조 탐색합니다. for (let c = Math.max(0, nameCol - 8); c <= Math.min(maxCol - 1, nameCol + 8); c++) { if (c === nameCol) continue; if (adminColumnHasTargetDateHeader_(values, c, rowIndex, dateInfo)) return c; } return -1; } function adminColumnHasTargetDateHeader_(values, colIndex, nearRow, dateInfo) { const start = Math.max(0, nearRow - 16); const end = Math.min(values.length - 1, nearRow + 2); for (let r = start; r <= end; r++) { const text = String((values[r] || [])[colIndex] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!text) continue; if (dateInfo.patterns.indexOf(text) !== -1) return true; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.m + "/" + dateInfo.d) !== -1) return true; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.mm + "/" + dateInfo.dd) !== -1) return true; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.m + "월" + dateInfo.d + "일") !== -1) return true; if (text.indexOf(dateInfo.d + "일") !== -1 && /월|일|주차|요일/.test(text)) return true; } return false; } function adminBuildDateInfoForAttendanceWrite_(dateText) { const text = String(dateText || "").trim(); let m = text.match(/^(\d{4})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})$/); if (!m) { const parsed = new Date(text); if (!isNaN(parsed.getTime())) { m = [ "", String(parsed.getFullYear()), String(parsed.getMonth() + 1), String(parsed.getDate()) ]; } } if (!m) return null; const year = Number(m[1]); const month = Number(m[2]); const day = Number(m[3]); if (!year || !month || !day) return null; const mm = String(month).padStart(2, "0"); const dd = String(day).padStart(2, "0"); let existingInfo = null; try { if (typeof getDateInfo_ === "function") existingInfo = getDateInfo_(dateText); } catch (ignore) {} const patterns = [ month + "/" + day, mm + "/" + dd, month + "월" + day + "일", month + "월 " + day + "일", day + "일", String(day) ].map(function(v) { return String(v).replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); }); if (existingInfo && existingInfo.patterns && existingInfo.patterns.length) { existingInfo.patterns.forEach(function(v) { const p = String(v || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (p && patterns.indexOf(p) === -1) patterns.push(p); }); } return { year: year, month: month, day: day, m: String(month), d: String(day), mm: mm, dd: dd, patterns: patterns }; } function adminAttendanceTargetScopeMatches_(record, className, instructor, sheetName, allowLooseInstructorOnly) { const targetClass = normalizeForLooseMatch_(record.className || ""); } } // 반명이 없는 레코드는 강사 시트 기준으로 허용합니다. if (!targetClass && targetInstructor && blockInstructor && targetInstructor === blockInstructor) return true; // 관리자 전체조회 등에서 반명/강사가 비어 들어온 경우를 위한 최소 허용 if (!targetClass && !targetInstructor) return true; return false; } function adminCanWriteAttendanceRecord_(admin, record) { try { if (typeof attendanceRecordBelongsToAdmin_ === "function") { return attendanceRecordBelongsToAdmin_(record, admin); } } catch (ignore) {} const role = String(admin && admin.role || ""); } } catch (ignore) {} const m = String(sheetName || "").match(/([가-힣]{2,4})\s*T?/); return m ? m[1] : ""; } function adminColumnToLetter_(col) { let temp = ""; let n = Number(col); while (n > 0) { const rem = (n - 1) % 26; temp = String.fromCharCode(65 + rem) + temp; n = Math.floor((n - rem) / 26); } return temp; } function appendWebAttendanceRecords_(records, admin) { // 의도적으로 비활성화: 출석 기록은 기존 출석부 시트만 원본으로 사용합니다. return; } if (String(info.actionType || "").toLowerCase() === "change" || String(info.actionType || "") === "변경") { return "안녕하세요. 울림연기학원입니다.\n\n" + studentName + " 학생의 연습실 예약 변경 안내입니다.\n\n" + "기존 예약: " + date + " " + time + " / " + room + "\n" + "변경 예약: " + newDate + " " + newTime + " / " + newRoom + "\n" + "현관 비밀번호: " + pw + "\n\n" + "변경된 내용 확인 후 이용 부탁드립니다.\n\n" + "울림연기학원"; } return "안녕하세요. 울림연기학원입니다.\n\n" + studentName + " 학생의 연습실 예약이 확인되었습니다.\n\n" + "예약일: " + date + "\n" + "예약시간: " + time + "\n" + "연습실: " + room + "\n" + "현관 비밀번호: " + pw + "\n\n" + "예약 시간에 맞춰 이용 부탁드립니다.\n\n" + "울림연기학원"; } function getRoomDoorPassword_() { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const propValue = String(props.getProperty("ROOM_DOOR_PASSWORD") || props.getProperty("ROOM_ENTRANCE_PASSWORD") || "").trim(); if (propValue) return propValue; try { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ROOM_RESERVATION_SPREADSHEET_ID); const candidates = [ ss.getSheetByName(ROOM_RESERVATION_CONFIG_SHEET_NAME), ss.getSheetByName("설정"), ss.getSheetByName("연습실 설정"), ss.getSheetByName("비밀번호") ].filter(Boolean); for (let i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) { const value = scanRoomPasswordSheet_(candidates[i]); if (value) return value; } const sheets = ss.getSheets(); for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) { const value = scanRoomPasswordSheet_(sheets[i]); if (value) return value; } } catch (err) { return ""; } return ""; } function scanRoomPasswordSheet_(sheet) { if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 1 || sheet.getLastColumn() < 1) return ""; const rowCount = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 50); const colCount = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 20); const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, rowCount, colCount).getDisplayValues(); // 현재 연습실예약 시트의 [설정] 구조 대응: // 예) A열: 현관비밀번호 / C열: 1130 처럼 값이 바로 오른쪽 칸이 아니라 같은 행의 다른 칸에 있어도 읽습니다. const keyPattern = /(현관|입구|출입|도어락|door|entrance).*(비밀|비번|password|pw)|^(비밀번호|비번)$/i; const passwordLike = /^[0-9#*]{3,12}$/; for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) { for (let c = 0; c < values[r].length; c++) { const cell = String(values[r][c] || "").trim(); if (!cell) continue; if (keyPattern.test(cell.replace(/\s/g, ""))) { // 1) 같은 행의 오른쪽 칸들을 먼저 탐색 for (let cc = c + 1; cc < values[r].length; cc++) { const rightValue = String(values[r][cc] || "").trim(); if (rightValue && passwordLike.test(rightValue.replace(/\s/g, ""))) { return rightValue; } } // 2) 바로 아래 같은 열 탐색 const below = values[r + 1] ? String(values[r + 1][c] || "").trim() : ""; if (below && passwordLike.test(below.replace(/\s/g, ""))) { return below; } // 3) 아래 행 오른쪽 주변 칸까지 탐색 if (values[r + 1]) { for (let cc = c + 1; cc < values[r + 1].length; cc++) { const belowRight = String(values[r + 1][cc] || "").trim(); if (belowRight && passwordLike.test(belowRight.replace(/\s/g, ""))) { return belowRight; } } } } } } return ""; } function readRoomReservationsForAdmin_(targetDate, year, month) { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ROOM_RESERVATION_SPREADSHEET_ID); const sheet = findRoomReservationDataSheet_(ss); if (!sheet) throw new Error("연습실 예약 데이터 시트를 찾지 못했습니다."); const values = sheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues(); if (!values || values.length < 2) return []; const headerRow = findRoomReservationHeaderRow_(values); if (headerRow < 0) return []; const headers = values[headerRow] || []; const col = { id: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["예약ID", "예약 ID", "id", "고유ID", "고유번호"], -1), date: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["예약일", "사용일", "날짜", "일자", "date"], -1), name: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["학생명", "예약자", "사용자", "이름", "성명", "student"], -1), phoneLast4: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["전화뒷자리", "휴대폰뒷자리", "뒤4자리", "phoneLast4", "출결번호"], -1), studentPhone: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["학생전화", "연락처", "전화번호", "휴대폰", "phone"], -1), room: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["연습실", "강의실", "장소", "룸", "room"], -1), start: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["시작시간", "시작", "startHour", "start", "시간"], -1), end: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["종료시간", "종료", "endHour", "end", "끝"], -1), status: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["상태", "예약상태", "처리상태", "status"], -1), memo: findRoomColumn_(headers, ["메모", "비고", "사유", "memo", "note"], -1) }; if (col.date < 0 || col.name < 0 || col.room < 0) { throw new Error("연습실 예약 시트의 헤더를 인식하지 못했습니다. 예약일/학생명/연습실 헤더가 필요합니다."); } const out = []; for (let r = headerRow + 1; r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const dateKey = dailyEvalDateKey_(row[col.date] || ""); const studentName = String(row[col.name] || "").trim(); const room = String(row[col.room] || "").trim(); if (!dateKey || !studentName || !room) continue; String(row[col.status] || "").trim() : "예약"; if (status === "취소") continue; const startRaw = col.start >= 0 ? row[col.start] : ""; const endRaw = col.end >= 0 ? row[col.end] : ""; out.push({ id: col.id >= 0 ? String(row[col.id] || "").trim() : String(r + 1), rowNumber: r + 1, date: dateKey, studentName: studentName, name: studentName, phoneLast4: col.phoneLast4 >= 0 ? String(row[col.studentPhone] || "").trim() : "", room: room, roomName: room, startHour: roomHourNumber_(startRaw), endHour: roomHourNumber_(endRaw), time: buildRoomTimeText_(roomHourText_(startRaw), roomHourText_(endRaw), String(startRaw || "")), status: status || "예약", memo: col.memo >= 0 ? String(row[col.memo] || "").trim() : "" }); } return out; } function findRoomReservationDataSheet_(ss) { const sheets = ss.getSheets(); for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) { if (Number(sheets[i].getSheetId()) === Number(ROOM_RESERVATION_TARGET_GID)) return sheets[i]; } const nameCandidates = ["연습실예약", "연습실 예약", "연습실사용일지", "예약목록", "예약DB"]; for (let i = 0; i < nameCandidates.length; i++) { const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(nameCandidates[i]); if (sheet) return sheet; } for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) { const values = sheets[i].getRange(1, 1, Math.min(10, sheets[i].getLastRow()), Math.min(20, sheets[i].getLastColumn())).getDisplayValues(); if (findRoomReservationHeaderRow_(values) >= 0) return sheets[i]; } return null; } function findRoomReservationHeaderRow_(values) { const maxRows = Math.min(values.length, 15); for (let r = 0; r < maxRows; r++) { const joined = (values[r] || []).map(function(v) { return normalizeHeader_(v); }).join("|"); const hasDate = joined.indexOf("예약일") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("사용일") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("날짜") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("일자") !== -1; const hasName = joined.indexOf("학생명") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("예약자") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("사용자") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("이름") !== -1; const hasRoom = joined.indexOf("연습실") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("강의실") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("장소") !== -1 || joined.indexOf("room") !== -1; if (hasDate && hasName && hasRoom) return r; } return -1; } function findRoomColumn_(headers, candidates, fallbackIndex) { return findStudentColumnByHeader_(headers, candidates, fallbackIndex); } function roomHourNumber_(value) { const text = String(value || "").trim(); if (!text) return ""; const m = text.match(/(\d{1,2})(?::\d{2})?/); return m ? Number(m[1]) : ""; } function roomHourText_(value) { const h = roomHourNumber_(value); if (h === "" || h === null || h === undefined || Number.isNaN(Number(h))) return ""; return String(Number(h)).padStart(2, "0") + ":00"; } function buildRoomTimeText_(startText, endText, fallback) { let start = roomHourText_(startText); let end = roomHourText_(endText); const raw = String(fallback || "").trim(); if ((!start || !end) && raw) { const matches = raw.match(/\d{1,2}(?::\d{2})?/g) || []; if (!start && matches[0]) start = roomHourText_(matches[0]); if (!end && matches[1]) end = roomHourText_(matches[1]); } if (start && end) return start + "~" + end; if (start) return start; return raw || ""; } function dailyEvalDateKey_(value) { if (!value) return ""; if (Object.prototype.toString.call(value) === "[object Date]") { return Utilities.formatDate(value, "Asia/Seoul", "yyyy-MM-dd"); } const text = String(value || "").trim(); } function adminGetDailyEvaluations_(params) { try { const admin = requireAdmin_(params); const targetDate = dailyEvalDateKey_(params.date || ""); const targetClass = String(params.className || "").trim(); } catch (err) { return jsonOutput_({ status: "error", message: err.message }); } } function buildMessagesForRecords_(records, recipientTypes, type, textBuilder, admin) { const instructorMap = getInstructorPhoneMap_(); const adminPhones = getAdminPhones_(); const messages = []; function pushMessage_(record, to, receiverType, text) { const phone = normalizePhone_(to); if (!phone || !text) return; messages.push(Object.assign({}, record || {}, { to: phone, studentName: String((record && record.studentName) || "").trim(), receiverType: receiverType, target: receiverType, messageType: type, text: text })); } records.forEach(r => { const text = textBuilder(r); const studentName = String(r.studentName || "").trim(); const sPhone = normalizePhone_(r.studentPhone); const pPhone = normalizePhone_(r.parentPhone); const instructorName = normalizeName(r.instructor || ""); const iPhone = normalizePhone_(instructorMap[instructorName]); if (recipientTypes.indexOf("학생") !== -1 && sPhone) pushMessage_(r, sPhone, "학생", text); if (recipientTypes.indexOf("학부모") !== -1 && pPhone && pPhone !== sPhone) pushMessage_(r, pPhone, "학부모", text); if (recipientTypes.indexOf("강사") !== -1 && iPhone) pushMessage_(r, iPhone, "강사", text); if (recipientTypes.indexOf("관리자") !== -1) { adminPhones.forEach(phone => pushMessage_(r, phone, "관리자", text));
