} function onSpecialAttendanceEdit_(e) { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(3000)) return; try { if (!e || !e.range) return; const range = e.range; if (range.getNumRows() !== 1 || range.getNumColumns() !== 1) return; const sheet = range.getSheet(); const parent = sheet.getParent(); if (!parent || parent.getId() !== ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID) return; const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (sheetName === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록)/.test(sheetName)) return; const newText = String(e.value || range.getDisplayValue() || "").trim(); const oldText = String(e.oldValue || "").trim(); const newType = normalizeSpecialAttendanceType_(newText); const oldType = normalizeSpecialAttendanceType_(oldText); if (!newType && !oldType) return; const record = buildSpecialAttendanceRecordFromEditedCell_(sheet, range); if (!record) return; if (newType) { record.type = newType; // 문자템플릿 시트의 [발송시각] 값을 기준으로 예약 시간을 다시 계산합니다. record.scheduledAt = getSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(record.classDate, newType); upsertSpecialAttendanceQueue_(record); } else { cancelSpecialAttendanceQueue_(record, oldType || ""); } } catch (err) { logSpecialAttendanceError_("onEdit", err); } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } /** * v44 추가: * 기존 v43은 날짜 출결칸에 "신규/보강/반이동"이라는 텍스트가 입력될 때만 onEdit로 감지했습니다. * 실제 출석부 운영처럼 이름칸 배경색(노랑=신규, 초록=보강, 보라=반이동)으로 표시하는 경우를 위해 * 전체 출석부를 주기적으로 스캔해서 예약문자대기열에 등록합니다. */ function scanSpecialAttendanceMarkedStudents() { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) return; try { setupSpecialAttendanceMessageSheetsWithoutAlert_(); // v61: 출석부 전체 스캔은 하루 1회만 허용합니다. // 설치된 트리거가 여러 개 남아 있거나 수동 실행을 여러 번 눌러도 중복 스캔을 막습니다. const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const todayKey = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_SCAN_TIMEZONE, "yyyy-MM-dd"); const lastScanKey = String(props.getProperty(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_LAST_SCAN_PROP) || "").trim(); if (lastScanKey === todayKey) { logSpecialAttendanceScanResult_(0, "SKIP_ALREADY_SCANNED_TODAY"); return; } props.setProperty(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_LAST_SCAN_PROP, todayKey); const attendanceSS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(ATTENDANCE_SHEET_ID); let added = 0; attendanceSS.getSheets().forEach(function(sheet) { const sheetName = sheet.getName(); if (sheetName === WEB_ATTENDANCE_SHEET_NAME) return; if (/^(보관|백업|숨김|공지|설정|웹출석기록)/.test(sheetName)) return; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 180); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 26); if (lastRow < 5 || lastCol < 2) return; const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol); const values = range.getDisplayValues(); const backgrounds = range.getBackgrounds(); const blocks = findSpecialAttendanceBlocksForScan_(values, sheetName); blocks.forEach(function(block) { for (let r = block.headerRow + 1; r <= block.blockEnd && r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; const studentName = String(row[block.panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); if (!isNameCellLikeStudent_(studentName)) continue; const nameBg = String((backgrounds[r] || [])[block.panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); const nameType = normalizeSpecialAttendanceColorType_(nameBg); if (nameType) { const dateCol = findFirstFutureSpecialAttendanceDateCol_(values, block); if (dateCol >= 0) { const record = buildSpecialAttendanceRecordFromBlock_(sheet, values, backgrounds, block, r, dateCol, nameType); if (record && upsertSpecialAttendanceQueue_(record) === true) { added++; } } } // 날짜칸 자체를 색 또는 텍스트로 표시한 경우도 보조 감지합니다. // 단, buildSpecialAttendanceRecordFromBlock_에서 오늘 이전 수업일은 다시 차단합니다. for (let c = block.panel.nameCol + 1; c < block.panel.memoCol && c < lastCol; c++) { const cellText = String(row[c] || "").trim(); const cellBg = String((backgrounds[r] || [])[c] || "").trim(); const type = normalizeSpecialAttendanceType_(cellText) || normalizeSpecialAttendanceColorType_(cellBg); if (!type) continue; const record = buildSpecialAttendanceRecordFromBlock_(sheet, values, backgrounds, block, r, c, type); if (record && upsertSpecialAttendanceQueue_(record) === true) { added++; } } } }); }); logSpecialAttendanceScanResult_(added, "DONE"); } catch (err) { logSpecialAttendanceError_("scan", err); } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function resetSpecialAttendanceDailyScanLock() { PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_LAST_SCAN_PROP); SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("✅ 신규/보강/반이동 하루 1회 스캔 잠금을 초기화했습니다.\n필요할 때만 수동으로 실행하세요."); } function findSpecialAttendanceBlocksForScan_(values, sheetName) { const blocks = []; const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); const panels = getAttendanceMonthPanelsForDate_(values, { valid: false }); for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) { if (normalizeHeader_(row[c]) !== "이름") continue; const panel = getPanelForNameCol_(panels, c); if (!panel) continue; const classText = findClassTextInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel); if (!classText) continue; const dayText = findDayTextInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel); const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, classText); const blockEnd = findStudentBlockEndAfterHeader_(values, r, panel); blocks.push({ panel: panel, headerRow: r, blockEnd: blockEnd, classText: classText, dayText: dayText, className: className, instructor: teacher.replace(/T$/, "") }); } } return blocks; } function normalizeSpecialAttendanceColorType_(color) { const rgb = parseHexColor_(color); if (!rgb) return ""; const r = rgb.r; const g = rgb.g; const b = rgb.b; // 흰색/회색/검정 계열 제외 if (r > 245 && g > 245 && b > 245) return ""; if (Math.abs(r - g) < 12 && Math.abs(g - b) < 12) return ""; // 노란색 = 신규 if (r >= 210 && g >= 190 && b <= 120) return "신규"; // 초록색 = 보강 if (g >= 145 && g >= r + 25 && g >= b + 20) return "보강"; // 보라색 = 반이동 if (b >= 125 && r >= 90 && b >= g + 15 && r >= g - 20) return "반이동"; return ""; } function parseHexColor_(color) { const text = String(color || "").trim(); const m = text.match(/^#?([0-9a-fA-F]{6})$/); if (!m) return null; const hex = m[1]; return { r: parseInt(hex.slice(0, 2), 16), g: parseInt(hex.slice(2, 4), 16), b: parseInt(hex.slice(4, 6), 16) }; } function findFirstFutureSpecialAttendanceDateCol_(values, block) { // v47: 이름칸 색상 스캔 시 오늘 이전 날짜는 절대 선택하지 않습니다. // 기존 버전은 미래 날짜가 없으면 첫 날짜칸으로 fallback되어 지난 날짜가 대기열에 들어갈 수 있었습니다. let firstFutureCol = -1; for (let c = block.panel.nameCol + 1; c < block.panel.memoCol && c < (values[block.headerRow] || []).length; c++) { const dateText = extractDateFromSpecialAttendanceColumn_(values, block.headerRow, block.panel, c); if (!dateText) continue; if (isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(dateText)) continue; firstFutureCol = c; break; } return firstFutureCol; } function buildSpecialAttendanceRecordFromBlock_(sheet, values, backgrounds, block, rowIndex, dateCol, type) { const row = values[rowIndex] || []; const rowStudentName = String(row[block.panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); if (!rowStudentName) return null; const classDate = extractDateFromSpecialAttendanceColumn_(values, block.headerRow, block.panel, dateCol); if (!classDate) return null; // 지난 수업일은 예약문자대기열에 등록하지 않음 if (isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(classDate)) return null; const scheduledAt = getSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(classDate, type); // 발송예정시각이 이미 지난 건은 새로 대기열에 넣지 않음 // 예: 전날17시 발송 규칙인데 당일/이후에 스캔된 과거 표시 if (isPastSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(scheduledAt)) return null; let studentName = rowStudentName; // 보강 날짜칸에는 행 학생명이 아니라 실제 보강 학생명이 적히는 경우가 있음. // 예: 김은혜 행의 보강칸에 "이재호"가 적혀 있으면 김은혜가 아니라 이재호로 처리. const cellText = String(row[dateCol] || "").trim(); const cellHasExplicitType = !!normalizeSpecialAttendanceType_(cellText); if (type === "보강" && cellText && !cellHasExplicitType) { const extracted = extractStudentNameFromSpecialCell_(cellText); if (extracted && isNameCellLikeStudent_(extracted)) { studentName = extracted; } } const monthText = getMonthTextFromDate_(classDate); const instructor = block.instructor || normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheet.getName()).replace(/T$/, ""); const className = block.className || ""; const classroom = resolveAttendanceClassroom_(classDate, className, instructor, "") || "데스크문의"; const studentMap = {}; getStudentsForAdmin_().forEach(function(student) { studentMap[student.nameKey] = student; }); const student = studentMap[normalizeName(studentName)] || makeFallbackStudent_(studentName, instructor); const instructorMap = getInstructorPhoneMap_(); const instructorPhone = instructorMap[normalizeName(instructor)] || instructorMap[normalizeName(instructor + "T")] || ""; return { type: type, classDate: classDate, monthText: monthText, scheduledAt: scheduledAt, studentName: studentName, className: className, classroom: classroom, instructor: instructor, studentPhone: student.studentPhone || "", parentPhone: student.parentPhone || "", instructorPhone: instructorPhone || "" }; } function logSpecialAttendanceScanResult_(added, status) { try { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); setupSheetWithHeaders_(ss, "예약문자스캔로그", ["일시", "등록건수", "상태"]); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("예약문자스캔로그"); sheet.appendRow([new Date(), added, status || "DONE"]); } catch (ignore) {} } function normalizeSpecialAttendanceType_(value) { const text = String(value || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!text) return ""; if (text.indexOf("반이동") !== -1 || text.indexOf("반변경") !== -1) return "반이동"; if (text.indexOf("신규") !== -1 || text.indexOf("첫수업") !== -1) return "신규"; if (text.indexOf("보강") !== -1) return "보강"; return ""; } function buildSpecialAttendanceRecordFromEditedCell_(sheet, range) { const rowIndex = range.getRow() - 1; const colIndex = range.getColumn() - 1; const lastRow = Math.min(sheet.getLastRow(), 180); const lastCol = Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 26); if (lastRow < 5 || lastCol < 2) return null; const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).getDisplayValues(); const block = findSpecialAttendanceBlockByEditedCell_(values, sheet.getName(), rowIndex, colIndex); if (!block) return null; const row = values[rowIndex] || []; let studentName = String(row[block.panel.nameCol] || "").trim(); if (!isNameCellLikeStudent_(studentName)) { studentName = extractStudentNameFromSpecialCell_(String(row[colIndex] || range.getDisplayValue() || "")); } if (!studentName) return null; const classDate = extractDateFromSpecialAttendanceColumn_(values, block.headerRow, block.panel, block.dateCol); if (!classDate) return null; // v47: 날짜칸 직접 입력도 지난 수업일이면 대기열에 등록하지 않음 if (isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(classDate)) return null; const monthText = getMonthTextFromDate_(classDate); const instructor = block.instructor || ""; const className = block.className || ""; const classroom = resolveAttendanceClassroom_(classDate, className, instructor, "") || "데스크문의"; const studentMap = {}; getStudentsForAdmin_().forEach(function(student) { studentMap[student.nameKey] = student; }); const student = studentMap[normalizeName(studentName)] || makeFallbackStudent_(studentName, instructor); const instructorMap = getInstructorPhoneMap_(); const instructorPhone = instructorMap[normalizeName(instructor)] || instructorMap[normalizeName(instructor + "T")] || ""; const scheduledAt = getSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(classDate); // 발송예정시각이 이미 지난 날짜칸 수정은 대기열에 넣지 않음 if (isPastSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(scheduledAt)) return null; return { type: "", classDate: classDate, monthText: monthText, scheduledAt: scheduledAt, studentName: studentName, className: className, classroom: classroom, instructor: instructor, studentPhone: student.studentPhone || "", parentPhone: student.parentPhone || "", instructorPhone: instructorPhone || "" }; } function findSpecialAttendanceBlockByEditedCell_(values, sheetName, rowIndex, colIndex) { const teacher = normalizeTeacherNameForClass_(sheetName); const panels = getAttendanceMonthPanelsForDate_(values, { valid: false }); for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) { if (normalizeHeader_(row[c]) !== "이름") continue; const panel = getPanelForNameCol_(panels, c); if (!panel) continue; const isDateCol = colIndex > panel.nameCol && colIndex < panel.memoCol; if (!isDateCol) continue; const blockEnd = findStudentBlockEndAfterHeader_(values, r, panel); if (rowIndex <= r || rowIndex > blockEnd) continue; const classText = findClassTextInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel); if (!classText) continue; const dayText = findDayTextInAttendancePanel_(values, r, panel); const className = formatClassNameFromAttendanceWithDay_(teacher, dayText, classText); const instructor = teacher.replace(/T$/, ""); return { panel: panel, headerRow: r, blockEnd: blockEnd, dateCol: colIndex, classText: classText, dayText: dayText, className: className, instructor: instructor }; } } return null; } function extractStudentNameFromSpecialCell_(text) { let value = String(text || "").trim(); value = value .replace(/반이동|반변경|신규|첫수업|보강|학생|수강생|추가|참여|예정/g, " ") .replace(/[\[\]()/,，:：\-]/g, " ") .replace(/\s+/g, " ") .trim(); const m = value.match(/[가-힣]{2,5}/); return m ? m[0] : ""; } function extractDateFromSpecialAttendanceColumn_(values, headerRow, panel, dateCol) { let year = ""; let month = ""; let day = ""; const startRow = Math.max(0, headerRow - 3); const endRow = Math.min(values.length - 1, headerRow + 1); for (let r = startRow; r <= endRow; r++) { const text = String((values[r] || [])[dateCol] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (!text) continue; let m = text.match(/(20\d{2})[-\/.년](\d{1,2})[-\/.월](\d{1,2})/); if (m) { year = m[1]; month = String(Number(m[2])); day = String(Number(m[3])); break; } m = text.match(/(\d{1,2})[\/.월](\d{1,2})/); if (m) { month = String(Number(m[1])); day = String(Number(m[2])); break; } m = text.match(/^(\d{1,2})일?$/); if (m) { day = String(Number(m[1])); } } if (!month) { month = findMonthInSpecialAttendancePanel_(values, headerRow, panel); } if (!day || !month) return ""; if (!year) { const now = new Date(); let y = now.getFullYear(); const nowMonth = now.getMonth() + 1; const mNum = Number(month); if (nowMonth === 12 && mNum === 1) y += 1; if (nowMonth === 1 && mNum === 12) y -= 1; year = String(y); } return year + "-" + String(Number(month)).padStart(2, "0") + "-" + String(Number(day)).padStart(2, "0"); } function findMonthInSpecialAttendancePanel_(values, headerRow, panel) { const startRow = 0; const endRow = Math.min(values.length - 1, Math.max(headerRow, 12)); let best = null; for (let r = startRow; r <= endRow; r++) { const row = values[r] || []; for (let c = panel.start; c <= panel.end && c < row.length; c++) { const text = String(row[c] || "").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); const m = text.match(/(\d{1,2})월/); if (!m) continue; const score = Math.abs(r - headerRow) * 10 + Math.abs(c - panel.nameCol); if (!best || score < best.score) { best = { month: String(Number(m[1])), score: score }; } } } return best ? best.month : ""; } function getMonthTextFromDate_(dateText) { const m = String(dateText || "").match(/^\d{4}-(\d{1,2})-/); return m ? String(Number(m[1])) + "월" : ""; } function getSpecialTodayDateKey_() { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "Asia/Seoul", "yyyy-MM-dd"); } function normalizeSpecialDateKey_(dateText) { const text = String(dateText || "").trim(); const m = text.match(/(20\d{2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})/); if (!m) return ""; return m[1] + "-" + String(Number(m[2])).padStart(2, "0") + "-" + String(Number(m[3])).padStart(2, "0"); } function isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(dateText) { const dateKey = normalizeSpecialDateKey_(dateText); if (!dateKey) return false; return dateKey < getSpecialTodayDateKey_(); } function isPastSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(scheduledAt) { if (!scheduledAt) return false; let d = scheduledAt; if (!(Object.prototype.toString.call(d) === "[object Date]" && !isNaN(d.getTime()))) { d = parseSpecialQueueDate_(scheduledAt); } if (!d || isNaN(d.getTime())) return false; const now = new Date(); // 1분 정도의 실행 지연은 허용하고, 그보다 이전이면 새 대기열 등록 금지 return d.getTime() < now.getTime() - 60 * 1000; } function getSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(classDate, type) { const rule = getSpecialAttendanceSendRule_(type); const parsed = parseSpecialAttendanceSendRule_(rule); if (parsed.mode === "now") { return new Date(); } const d = new Date(String(classDate || "") + "T00:00:00+09:00"); if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return new Date(); d.setDate(d.getDate() + parsed.dayOffset); d.setHours(parsed.hour, parsed.minute, 0, 0); return d; } function getSpecialAttendanceSendRule_(type) { setupSpecialAttendanceMessageSheetsWithoutAlert_(); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SPECIAL_SMS_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return "전날17시"; const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getDisplayValues(); // 같은 구분에서 학생용 발송시각을 우선 적용합니다. // 학생/강사 문자는 현재 한 대기열에서 같이 발송되므로, 같은 구분의 발송시각은 동일하게 맞춰두는 것을 권장합니다. let fallbackRule = ""; for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) { const row = values[i]; const active = String(row[0] || "").trim().toUpperCase(); const rowType = String(row[1] || "").trim(); const rowTarget = String(row[2] || "").trim(); const sendRule = String(row[3] || "").trim(); if (!(active === "TRUE" || active === "Y" || active === "사용" || active === "1")) continue; if (rowType !== type) continue; if (!sendRule) continue; if (!fallbackRule) fallbackRule = sendRule; if (rowTarget === "학생") return sendRule; } return fallbackRule || "전날17시"; } function parseSpecialAttendanceSendRule_(rule) { const text = String(rule || "전날17시").replace(/\s/g, "").trim(); if (/즉시|바로/.test(text)) { return { mode: "now", dayOffset: 0, hour: 0, minute: 0 }; } let dayOffset = -1; if (/당일|오늘|D0|D\+0/i.test(text)) { dayOffset = 0; } else { const dMinus = text.match(/D[-－](\d+)/i); const daysBefore = text.match(/(\d+)일전/); if (dMinus) { dayOffset = -Number(dMinus[1]); } else if (daysBefore) { dayOffset = -Number(daysBefore[1]); } else if (/전날|하루전|1일전/.test(text)) { dayOffset = -1; } } let hour = 17; let minute = 0; let timeMatch = text.match(/(\d{1,2})[:：](\d{1,2})/); if (timeMatch) { hour = Number(timeMatch[1]); minute = Number(timeMatch[2]); } else { timeMatch = text.match(/(\d{1,2})시(?:(\d{1,2})분?)?/); if (timeMatch) { hour = Number(timeMatch[1]); minute = timeMatch[2] ? Number(timeMatch[2]) : 0; } } if (isNaN(hour) || hour < 0 || hour > 23) hour = 17; if (isNaN(minute) || minute < 0 || minute > 59) minute = 0; return { mode: "scheduled", dayOffset: dayOffset, hour: hour, minute: minute }; } function makeSpecialAttendanceQueueKey_(record) { return [ record.type || "", record.classDate || "", normalizeName(record.studentName || ""), normalizeForLooseMatch_(record.className || "") ].join("|"); } function upsertSpecialAttendanceQueue_(record) { setupSpecialAttendanceMessageSheetsWithoutAlert_(); // 어떤 경로로 들어와도 오늘 이전 수업일 또는 이미 발송예정시각이 지난 건은 대기열에 넣지 않습니다. if ( !record || !record.classDate || isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(record.classDate) || isPastSpecialAttendanceScheduledAt_(record.scheduledAt) ) { return false; } const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_QUEUE_SHEET_NAME); const key = makeSpecialAttendanceQueueKey_(record); // v61 핵심: 실패/대기/완료/취소 상태와 관계없이 같은 중복키가 있으면 재등록하지 않습니다. // 기존 코드는 발송실패 행을 다시 "대기"로 덮어써서 무한 재발송 위험이 있었습니다. if (specialAttendanceQueueKeyExists_(sheet, key)) { return false; } const studentText = buildSpecialAttendanceTemplateMessage_(record.type, "학생", record); const teacherText = buildSpecialAttendanceTemplateMessage_(record.type, "강사", record); const rowValues = [ new Date(), record.scheduledAt, "대기", record.type, record.classDate, record.monthText, record.studentName, record.className, record.classroom, record.instructor, record.studentPhone, record.parentPhone, record.instructorPhone, studentText, teacherText, key, "", "" ]; sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, rowValues.length).setValues([rowValues]); return true; } function specialAttendanceQueueKeyExists_(sheet, key) { const target = String(key || "").trim(); if (!sheet || !target) return false; const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow(); if (lastRow < 2) return false; const keys = sheet.getRange(2, 16, lastRow - 1, 1).getDisplayValues(); for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) { if (String(keys[i][0] || "").trim() === target) { return true; } } return false; } function cancelSpecialAttendanceQueue_(record, oldType) { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_QUEUE_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return; const targetTypes = oldType ? [oldType] : SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_TYPES; const now = new Date(); const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 18).getDisplayValues(); values.forEach(function(row, idx) { const status = String(row[2] || "").trim(); const type = String(row[3] || "").trim(); const date = String(row[4] || "").trim(); const name = String(row[6] || "").trim(); const className = String(row[7] || "").trim(); if (status !== "대기") return; if (targetTypes.indexOf(type) === -1) return; if (date !== record.classDate) return; if (normalizeName(name) !== normalizeName(record.studentName)) return; if (normalizeForLooseMatch_(className) !== normalizeForLooseMatch_(record.className)) return; const rowNo = idx + 2; sheet.getRange(rowNo, 3).setValue("취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 17).setValue("출석부 상태 변경으로 자동 취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 18).setValue(now); }); } function buildSpecialAttendanceTemplateMessage_(type, target, record) { const template = getSpecialAttendanceTemplate_(type, target); return applySpecialAttendanceTemplateTokens_(template, record); } function getSpecialAttendanceTemplate_(type, target) { setupSpecialAttendanceMessageSheetsWithoutAlert_(); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SPECIAL_SMS_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return getFallbackSpecialAttendanceTemplate_(type, target); const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 5).getDisplayValues(); for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) { const row = values[i]; const active = String(row[0] || "").trim().toUpperCase(); const rowType = String(row[1] || "").trim(); const rowTarget = String(row[2] || "").trim(); const text = String(row[4] || "").trim(); if (!(active === "TRUE" || active === "Y" || active === "사용" || active === "1")) continue; if (rowType !== type) continue; if (rowTarget !== target) continue; if (text) return text; } return getFallbackSpecialAttendanceTemplate_(type, target); } function getFallbackSpecialAttendanceTemplate_(type, target) { if (target === "강사") { return "안녕하세요. 울림연기학원입니다.\n\n내일 수업에 [출결구분] 학생 [학생명] 학생이 참여 예정입니다.\n\n수업일 : [수업일]\n수업명 : [반명]\n강의실 : [강의실]\n\n확인 부탁드립니다.\n\n- 울림연기학원"; } if (type === "반이동") { return "안녕하세요. 울림연기학원입니다.\n\n[학생명] 학생의 [월] 첫 수업 안내드립니다.\n\n수업일 : [수업일]\n수업명 : [반명]\n강의실 : [강의실]\n\n변경된 수업 일정과 강의실을 확인하시고 수업 시간에 맞춰 참석해 주세요.\n\n- 울림연기학원"; } return "안녕하세요. 울림연기학원입니다.\n\n[학생명] 학생의 [출결구분] 수업 안내드립니다.\n\n수업일 : [수업일]\n수업명 : [반명]\n강의실 : [강의실]\n\n수업 시간에 맞춰 참석해 주세요.\n\n- 울림연기학원"; } function applySpecialAttendanceTemplateTokens_(template, record) { const classroomText = normalizeClassroomFallbackText_(record.classroom); return String(template || "") .replace(/\[학생명\]/g, record.studentName || "") .replace(/\[월\]/g, record.monthText || getMonthTextFromDate_(record.classDate) || "") .replace(/\[수업일\]/g, record.classDate || "") .replace(/\[반명\]/g, record.className || "미확인") .replace(/\[수업명\]/g, record.className || "미확인") .replace(/\[강의실\]/g, classroomText) .replace(/\[담당강사\]/g, record.instructor || "") .replace(/\[출결구분\]/g, record.type || "") .replace(/\[학원명\]/g, "울림연기학원"); } function normalizeClassroomFallbackText_(classroom) { const text = String(classroom || "").trim(); if (!text || text === "미확인" || text === "확인 필요") return "데스크문의"; return text; } function normalizeOutgoingClassroomFallbackText_(message) { return String(message || "") .replace(/강의실\s*[:：]\s*(미확인|확인\s*필요)/g, "강의실 : 데스크문의") .replace(/\[(미확인|확인\s*필요)\]/g, "[데스크문의]"); } /**************************************************** * 46. 신규/보강/반이동 예약 안내 알림톡 발송 * - SOLAPI 알림톡 전용 발송 * - 템플릿 ID가 없거나 알림톡 발송 실패 시 SMS/LMS로 대체 발송하지 않음 * * 설정값 권장값: * - SOLAPI_KAKAO_PFID * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_STUDENT * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_TEACHER * * 세부 템플릿을 따로 쓰고 싶으면 아래 속성이 우선 적용됩니다. * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_NEW_STUDENT * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_NEW_TEACHER * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_MAKEUP_STUDENT * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_MAKEUP_TEACHER * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_TRANSFER_STUDENT * - SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_TRANSFER_TEACHER ****************************************************/ function sendSpecialAttendanceNotificationMessages_(messages) { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const pfId = String(props.getProperty("SOLAPI_KAKAO_PFID") || "").trim(); if (!messages || !messages.length) { return { sent: false, message: "알림톡 미발송: 발송 대상 없음" }; } if (!pfId) { return { sent: false, message: "알림톡 발송 설정이 완료되지 않았습니다. 관리자에게 문의해주세요." }; } let success = 0; const errors = []; messages.forEach(function(message) { const templateId = getSpecialAttendanceAlimtalkTemplateId_(message.type, message.target); if (!templateId) { errors.push((message.receiverType || "대상") + ": 신규/보강/반이동 알림톡 템플릿 ID 없음"); return; } try { sendSpecialAttendanceAlimtalk_(message, templateId, pfId); success++; } catch (err) { errors.push((message.receiverType || "대상") + ": " + err.message); } }); const parts = []; if (success) parts.push("알림톡 발송 " + success + "건"); if (errors.length) parts.push("확인필요: " + errors.join(" / ")); return { sent: success > 0 && errors.length < messages.length, message: parts.join(" / ") || "알림톡 발송 대상 없음" }; } function getSpecialAttendanceAlimtalkTemplateId_(type, target) { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const typeKey = getSpecialAttendanceTemplateTypeKey_(type); const targetKey = target === "강사" ? "TEACHER" : "STUDENT"; const candidates = [ "SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_" + typeKey + "_" + targetKey, "SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_" + targetKey, "SOLAPI_TEMPLATE_ID_SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE" ]; for (let i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) { const value = String(props.getProperty(candidates[i]) || "").trim(); if (value) return value; } return ""; } function getSpecialAttendanceTemplateTypeKey_(type) { const text = String(type || "").trim(); if (text === "신규") return "NEW"; if (text === "보강") return "MAKEUP"; if (text === "반이동") return "TRANSFER"; return "ATTENDANCE"; } function sendSpecialAttendanceAlimtalk_(message, templateId, pfId) { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const sender = normalizePhone_(props.getProperty("SOLAPI_SENDER") || ""); const receiver = normalizePhone_(message.to); if (!receiver) throw new Error("수신번호 없음"); if (!sender) throw new Error("발신번호 설정이 완료되지 않았습니다."); if (!templateId) throw new Error("알림톡 템플릿 ID 없음"); if (!pfId) throw new Error("알림톡 채널 설정이 완료되지 않았습니다."); const safeStudentName = String(message.studentName || "").trim(); const safeType = String(message.type || "").trim(); const safeMonth = String(message.monthText || "").trim(); const safeDate = String(message.classDate || "").trim(); const safeClassName = String(message.className || "").trim() || "미확인"; const safeClassroom = normalizeClassroomFallbackText_(message.classroom); const safePracticeRoom = ""; const safeReservationTime = ""; const safeStartTime = ""; const safeEndTime = ""; const safeDoorPassword = ""; const safeNewDate = ""; const safeNewRoom = ""; const safeNewTime = ""; const safeReason = ""; const safeInstructor = String(message.instructor || "").trim(); const safeTarget = String(message.target || "").trim(); const safeText = normalizeOutgoingClassroomFallbackText_(String(message.text || "").trim()); const payload = { message: { to: receiver, from: sender, text: safeText, kakaoOptions: { pfId: pfId, templateId: templateId, disableSms: true, variables: { "#{학생명}": safeStudentName, "#{월}": safeMonth, "#{수업일}": safeDate, "#{반명}": safeClassName, "#{수업명}": safeClassName, "#{강의실}": safeClassroom, "#{연습실}": safePracticeRoom, "#{예약일}": safeDate, "#{예약날짜}": safeDate, "#{예약시간}": safeReservationTime, "#{시작시간}": safeStartTime, "#{종료시간}": safeEndTime, "#{현관비밀번호}": safeDoorPassword, "#{비밀번호}": safeDoorPassword, "#{변경일}": safeNewDate, "#{변경날짜}": safeNewDate, "#{변경연습실}": safeNewRoom, "#{변경장소}": safeNewRoom, "#{변경시간}": safeNewTime, "#{사용불가사유}": safeReason, "#{사유}": safeReason, "#{담당강사}": safeInstructor, "#{출결구분}": safeType, "#{수신대상}": safeTarget, "#{안내문구}": safeText, "#{문구}": safeText } } } }; return sendSolapiSingleMessage_(payload); } function processSpecialAttendanceMessageQueue() { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) return; try { setupSpecialAttendanceMessageSheetsWithoutAlert_(); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_QUEUE_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return; const now = new Date(); const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 18).getValues(); const systemAdmin = { id: "AUTO", name: "자동발송", phone: "" }; values.forEach(function(row, idx) { const rowNo = idx + 2; const scheduledAt = parseSpecialQueueDate_(row[1]); const status = String(row[2] || "").trim(); const type = String(row[3] || "").trim(); const classDate = normalizeSpecialDateKey_(row[4]); const studentName = String(row[6] || "").trim(); const studentPhone = normalizePhone_(row[10]); const instructorPhone = normalizePhone_(row[12]); const studentText = normalizeOutgoingClassroomFallbackText_(String(row[13] || "").trim()); const teacherText = normalizeOutgoingClassroomFallbackText_(String(row[14] || "").trim()); if (status !== "대기") return; // v61: 수업일이 없거나 오늘 이전이면 발송하지 않고 자동 취소합니다. // 과거 날짜 대기열이 남아 있어도 이후 트리거에서 재발송되지 않습니다. if (!classDate || isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(classDate)) { sheet.getRange(rowNo, 3).setValue("취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 17).setValue(!classDate ? "수업일 누락 예약문자 자동 취소" : "지난 수업일 예약문자 자동 취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 18).setValue(now); return; } if (!scheduledAt || scheduledAt.getTime() > now.getTime()) return; const monthText = String(row[5] || "").trim() || getMonthTextFromDate_(classDate); const className = String(row[7] || "").trim(); const classroom = normalizeClassroomFallbackText_(String(row[8] || "").trim()); const instructor = String(row[9] || "").trim(); const messages = []; if (studentPhone && studentText) { messages.push({ to: studentPhone, studentName: studentName, receiverType: type + "/학생", target: "학생", type: type, monthText: monthText, classDate: classDate, className: className, classroom: classroom, instructor: instructor, text: studentText }); } if (instructorPhone && teacherText) { messages.push({ to: instructorPhone, studentName: studentName, receiverType: type + "/강사", target: "강사", type: type, monthText: monthText, classDate: classDate, className: className, classroom: classroom, instructor: instructor, text: teacherText }); } if (!messages.length) { sheet.getRange(rowNo, 3).setValue("발송실패"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 17).setValue("발송 가능한 학생/강사 전화번호가 없습니다."); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 18).setValue(now); return; } const sendResult = sendSpecialAttendanceNotificationMessages_(messages); appendSmsLogs_(type + "예약안내", messages, sendResult, systemAdmin); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 3).setValue(sendResult.sent ? "발송완료" : "발송실패"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 17).setValue(sendResult.message || ""); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 18).setValue(new Date()); }); } catch (err) { logSpecialAttendanceError_("queue", err); } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function cleanupSpecialAttendanceQueueSafety() { // 이미 생성된 예약문자대기열을 안전하게 정리하는 수동 실행용 함수입니다. // 1) 오늘 이전 수업일의 대기 건은 취소 // 2) 같은 중복키가 여러 행이면 가장 먼저 나온 행만 남기고 나머지 대기 건은 중복취소 setupSpecialAttendanceMessageSheetsWithoutAlert_(); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SPECIAL_ATTENDANCE_QUEUE_SHEET_NAME); if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return; const now = new Date(); const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 18).getDisplayValues(); const seen = {}; let cancelledPast = 0; let cancelledDup = 0; values.forEach(function(row, idx) { const rowNo = idx + 2; const status = String(row[2] || "").trim(); const classDate = normalizeSpecialDateKey_(row[4]); const key = String(row[15] || "").trim(); if (status === "대기" && (!classDate || isPastSpecialAttendanceClassDate_(classDate))) { sheet.getRange(rowNo, 3).setValue("취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 17).setValue(!classDate ? "수업일 누락 안전정리 취소" : "지난 수업일 안전정리 취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 18).setValue(now); cancelledPast++; return; } if (!key) return; if (seen[key] && status === "대기") { sheet.getRange(rowNo, 3).setValue("취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 17).setValue("중복키 안전정리 취소"); sheet.getRange(rowNo, 18).setValue(now); cancelledDup++; return; } seen[key] = true; }); SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert( "✅ 예약문자대기열 안전정리 완료\n\n" + "지난/누락 수업일 취소: " + cancelledPast + "건\n" + "중복 대기 취소: " + cancelledDup + "건" ); } function parseSpecialQueueDate_(value) { if (!value) return null; if (Object.prototype.toString.call(value) === "[object Date]" && !isNaN(value.getTime())) return value; const text = String(value || "").trim(); if (!text) return null; const d = new Date(text); if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) return d; const m = text.match(/(20\d{2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2}).*?(\d{1,2}):(\d{1,2})/); if (m) { return new Date( Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3]), Number(m[4]), Number(m[5]), 0 ); } return null; } function logSpecialAttendanceError_(where, err) { try { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); setupSheetWithHeaders_(ss, "예약문자오류로그", ["일시", "위치", "오류"]); const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("예약문자오류로그"); sheet.appendRow([new Date(), where, err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)]); } catch (ignore) {} } function fixDailyEvalColumnWidths() { fixDailyEvalColumnWidths_(); SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("✅ 일일평가 열너비 고정 완료\n\n- 일일평가문구 B열: 440\n- 일일평가 I~M열: 보기 좋게 고정"); } function fixDailyEvalColumnWidths_() { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(STUDENT_SHEET_ID); // 일일평가문구 시트: B열 문구 칸 고정 const templateSheet = ss.getSheetByName(DAILY_EVAL_TEMPLATE_SHEET_NAME || "일일평가문구"); if (templateSheet) { templateSheet.setColumnWidth(1, 110); // A열 구분 templateSheet.setColumnWidth(2, 440); // B열 문구 templateSheet.getRange("A:B").setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP); templateSheet.getRange("A:B").setVerticalAlignment("middle"); } // 일일평가 시트: 3분리 입력 구조 기준 열너비 고정 const evalSheet = ss.getSheetByName(DAILY_EVAL_SHEET_NAME || "일일평가"); if (evalSheet) { const widths = { 1: 150, // 저장일시 2: 110, // 수업일 3: 220, // 반명 4: 110, // 학생명 5: 110, // 담당강사 6: 140, // 학생전화 7: 140, // 학부모전화 8: 90, // 출석여부 9: 260, // 수업내용 10: 260, // 수업태도 11: 260, // 전달사항 12: 300, // 수업영상링크 13: 440, // 일일평가 14: 130, // 문자발송결과 15: 110, // 관리자ID 16: 110 // 관리자명 }; Object.keys(widths).forEach(function(col) { evalSheet.setColumnWidth(Number(col), widths[col]); }); const maxRows = Math.max(evalSheet.getMaxRows(), 2); evalSheet.getRange(1, 1, maxRows, 16) .setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP) .setVerticalAlignment("middle"); evalSheet.setFrozenRows(1); evalSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.min(evalSheet.getLastColumn(), 16)) .setFontWeight("bold") .setBackground("#1F4E3D") .setFontColor("#ffffff") .setHorizontalAlignment("center"); } } /**************************************************** * 31-A. 로컬 AI 전환 안내 * - 일반분석 STT는 index.html 안의 브라우저 로컬 AI가 처리합니다. * - OpenAI API / OPENAI_API_KEY / whisperTranscribe GAS action은 더 이상 사용하지 않습니다. * - GAS는 AI 고급분석, 사용량 제한, 기존 연습일지/Drive 업로드 흐름만 담당합니다. ****************************************************/ /**************************************************** * 31. 울림앱 표준발음 탭 - AI 고급분석 고급분석 * - 학생부 스프레드시트에는 새 시트를 만들지 않음 * - ETRI_DATA_SPREADSHEET_ID 속성에 등록한 별도 스프레드시트에 사용량/로그 저장 * - ETRI_ACCESS_KEY는 스크립트 속성에만 저장해서 index.html에 노출하지 않음 * - 학생/기기 기준 하루 10회 제한 * - POST 제출 후 GET(JSONP)으로 결과 조회 ****************************************************/ const ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_API_URL = 'http://epretx.etri.re.kr:8000/api/WiseASR_PronunciationKor'; const ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_API_URL_PROP = 'ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_API_URL'; const ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_API_URL_FALLBACKS = [ 'http://epretx.etri.re.kr:8000/api/WiseASR_PronunciationKor', 'https://epretx.etri.re.kr:8000/api/WiseASR_PronunciationKor', 'https://epretx.etri.re.kr/api/WiseASR_PronunciationKor' ]; const ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT = 10; const ETRI_RESULT_CACHE_SECONDS = 21600; // 6시간 const ETRI_DATA_SPREADSHEET_ID_PROP = 'ETRI_DATA_SPREADSHEET_ID'; const ETRI_USAGE_SHEET_NAME = 'ETRI_사용량'; const ETRI_LOG_SHEET_NAME = 'ETRI_분석로그'; const ETRI_USAGE_HEADERS = [ 'dateKey', 'userKey', 'used', 'updatedAt' ]; const ETRI_LOG_HEADERS = [ 'createdAt', 'dateKey', 'requestId', 'userKey', 'studentName', 'phoneLast4', 'script', 'recognized', 'score', 'status', 'message' ]; function handleEtriPronunciationPost_(payload) { payload = payload || {}; const requestId = sanitizeEtriKey_(payload.requestId || makeEtriRequestId_()); const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); const userKey = sanitizeEtriKey_(payload.userKey || 'guest'); const dateKey = sanitizeEtriDateKey_(payload.dateKey || getKoreaDateKey_()); const studentName = String(payload.studentName || '').trim(); const phoneLast4 = String(payload.phoneLast4 || '').trim(); cache.put(resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId), JSON.stringify({ ok: true, status: 'pending', requestId: requestId, message: 'AI 고급분석 처리 대기 중입니다.' }), ETRI_RESULT_CACHE_SECONDS); const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); try { lock.waitLock(10000); const usage = getEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey); if (usage.used >= ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT) { const limited = { ok: false, status: 'limit', requestId: requestId, used: usage.used, remaining: 0, limit: ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT, message: '오늘 고급분석 10회를 모두 사용했습니다. 내일 다시 이용해주세요.' }; cache.put(resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId), JSON.stringify(limited), ETRI_RESULT_CACHE_SECONDS); appendEtriLog_({ dateKey: dateKey, requestId: requestId, userKey: userKey, studentName: studentName, phoneLast4: phoneLast4, script: String(payload.script || '').trim(), recognized: '', score: '', status: 'limit', message: limited.message }); return jsonOutput_(limited); } // 같은 requestId가 이미 완료된 경우에는 ETRI를 다시 호출하지 않고 캐시 결과를 그대로 반환합니다. const existingCachedResult = cache.get(resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId)); if (existingCachedResult) { try { const existingParsed = JSON.parse(existingCachedResult); if (existingParsed && existingParsed.status === 'done') { return jsonOutput_(existingParsed); } } catch (ignoreExistingResultErr) {} } const requestDedupKey = 'ETRI_REQ_' + requestId; const isDuplicateRequest = !!cache.get(requestDedupKey); if (!isDuplicateRequest) { cache.put(requestDedupKey, '1', ETRI_RESULT_CACHE_SECONDS); } const script = String(payload.script || '').trim(); const audio = String(payload.audio || '').trim(); if (!script) { throw new Error('제시 문장이 비어 있습니다.'); } if (!audio) { throw new Error('오디오 데이터가 비어 있습니다.'); } if (script.length > 1000) { throw new Error('제시 문장이 너무 깁니다. 문장을 짧게 나누어 평가해주세요.'); } const etriResult = callEtriPronunciationApi_(script, audio); const parsed = parseEtriReturnObject_(etriResult); // 중요: ETRI 서버 호출이 실제로 성공한 뒤에만 사용량을 1회 차감합니다. // 주소 접근 실패, 서버 장애, API 오류는 학생의 하루 10회 제한에서 차감하지 않습니다. if (!isDuplicateRequest) { setEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey, usage.used + 1); } const afterUsage = getEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey); const result = { ok: true, status: 'done', requestId: requestId, used: afterUsage.used, remaining: Math.max(0, ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT - afterUsage.used), limit: ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT, recognized: parsed.recognized || '', score: parsed.score || '', etri: parsed, raw: etriResult, message: 'AI 고급분석이 완료되었습니다.' }; appendEtriLog_({ dateKey: dateKey, requestId: requestId, userKey: userKey, studentName: studentName, phoneLast4: phoneLast4, script: script, recognized: result.recognized, score: result.score, status: 'done', message: result.message }); cache.put(resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId), JSON.stringify(result), ETRI_RESULT_CACHE_SECONDS); return jsonOutput_(result); } catch (err) { const usageAfterError = getEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey); const message = 'AI 고급분석 실패: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err); const errorResult = { ok: false, status: 'error', requestId: requestId, used: usageAfterError.used || 0, remaining: Math.max(0, ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT - (usageAfterError.used || 0)), limit: ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT, message: message }; appendEtriLog_({ dateKey: dateKey, requestId: requestId, userKey: userKey, studentName: studentName, phoneLast4: phoneLast4, script: String(payload.script || '').trim(), recognized: '', score: '', status: 'error', message: message }); cache.put(resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId), JSON.stringify(errorResult), ETRI_RESULT_CACHE_SECONDS); return jsonOutput_(errorResult); } finally { try { lock.releaseLock(); } catch (e) {} } } function handleGetEtriPronunciationResult_(e) { const requestId = sanitizeEtriKey_(e && e.parameter ? e.parameter.requestId || '' : ''); if (!requestId) { return jsonpOutput_(e, { ok: false, status: 'error', message: 'requestId가 없습니다.' }); } const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); const cached = cache.get(resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId)); if (!cached) { return jsonpOutput_(e, { ok: true, status: 'not_found', requestId: requestId, message: '아직 결과가 없습니다.' }); } try { return jsonpOutput_(e, JSON.parse(cached)); } catch (err) { return jsonpOutput_(e, { ok: false, status: 'error', requestId: requestId, message: '결과 파싱 실패' }); } } function handleGetEtriPronunciationUsage_(e) { const params = e && e.parameter ? e.parameter : {}; const userKey = sanitizeEtriKey_(params.userKey || 'guest'); const dateKey = sanitizeEtriDateKey_(params.dateKey || getKoreaDateKey_()); const usage = getEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey); return jsonpOutput_(e, { ok: true, status: 'done', userKey: userKey, dateKey: dateKey, used: usage.used, remaining: Math.max(0, ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT - usage.used), limit: ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_DAILY_LIMIT }); } function callEtriPronunciationApi_(script, audioBase64) { const accessKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ETRI_ACCESS_KEY'); if (!accessKey) { throw new Error('고급분석 설정이 완료되지 않았습니다. 일반분석으로 대체합니다.'); } const requestBody = { request_id: 'reserved field', argument: { language_code: 'korean', script: script, audio: audioBase64 } }; const apiUrls = getEtriPronunciationApiUrls_(); const errors = []; for (let i = 0; i < apiUrls.length; i++) { const url = apiUrls[i]; try { const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { method: 'post', contentType: 'application/json; charset=UTF-8', headers: { Authorization: accessKey }, payload: JSON.stringify(requestBody), muteHttpExceptions: true }); const status = response.getResponseCode(); const body = response.getContentText('UTF-8'); let data; try { data = JSON.parse(body); } catch (err) { throw new Error('응답 JSON 파싱 실패: HTTP ' + status + ' / ' + body.slice(0, 200)); } if (status < 200 || status >= 300 || Number(data.result) !== 0) { throw new Error('외부 분석 서버 응답 오류: ' + status + ' / ' + body.slice(0, 500)); } data._used_api_url = url; return data; } catch (err) { errors.push(url + ' => ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err)); } } throw new Error( 'AI 고급분석 서버에 연결하지 못했습니다. 실패한 주소: ' + errors.join(' | ') + ' / 외부 분석 서버 연결이 원활하지 않습니다.' ); } function getEtriPronunciationApiUrls_() { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const customUrl = String(props.getProperty(ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_API_URL_PROP) || '').trim(); const list = []; if (customUrl) list.push(customUrl); ETRI_PRONUNCIATION_API_URL_FALLBACKS.forEach(function(url) { if (list.indexOf(url) === -1) list.push(url); }); return list; } function parseEtriReturnObject_(etriResult) { const obj = etriResult && etriResult.return_object ? etriResult.return_object : {}; let parsed = obj; if (typeof obj === 'string') { try { parsed = JSON.parse(obj); } catch (e) { parsed = { recognized: obj }; } } return { recognized: parsed.recognized || parsed.result || parsed.text || '', score: parsed.score || parsed.pronunciation_score || parsed.Score || '', return_object: parsed }; } /**************************************************** * 31-1. ETRI 분리 스프레드시트 저장 함수 ****************************************************/ function getEtriDataSpreadsheet_() { const id = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(ETRI_DATA_SPREADSHEET_ID_PROP); if (!id) { throw new Error('설정값 ' + ETRI_DATA_SPREADSHEET_ID_PROP + '가 설정되지 않았습니다. AI 고급분석 전용 스프레드시트 ID를 등록해주세요.'); } return SpreadsheetApp.openById(id); } function getOrCreateEtriSheet_(sheetName, headers) { const ss = getEtriDataSpreadsheet_(); let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName); if (!sheet) { sheet = ss.insertSheet(sheetName); } const currentHeader = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).getValues()[0]; const hasHeader = currentHeader.some(function(v) { return String(v || '').trim(); }); if (!hasHeader) { sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]); sheet.setFrozenRows(1); sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length) .setFontWeight('bold') .setBackground('#1F4E3D') .setFontColor('#ffffff') .setHorizontalAlignment('center'); } return sheet; } function getEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey) { const sheet = getOrCreateEtriSheet_(ETRI_USAGE_SHEET_NAME, ETRI_USAGE_HEADERS); const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow(); if (lastRow < 2) { return { used: 0 }; } const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, ETRI_USAGE_HEADERS.length).getValues(); const targetDate = sanitizeEtriDateKey_(dateKey); const targetUser = sanitizeEtriKey_(userKey); for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) { const rowDate = sanitizeEtriDateKey_(values[i][0]); const rowUser = sanitizeEtriKey_(values[i][1]); if (rowDate === targetDate && rowUser === targetUser) { return { used: Number(values[i][2] || 0) || 0, rowNumber: i + 2 }; } } return { used: 0 }; } function setEtriUsage_(userKey, dateKey, used) { const sheet = getOrCreateEtriSheet_(ETRI_USAGE_SHEET_NAME, ETRI_USAGE_HEADERS); const targetDate = sanitizeEtriDateKey_(dateKey); const targetUser = sanitizeEtriKey_(userKey); const safeUsed = Math.max(0, Number(used) || 0); const now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'Asia/Seoul', 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'); const current = getEtriUsage_(targetUser, targetDate); if (current.rowNumber) { sheet.getRange(current.rowNumber, 1, 1, 4).setValues([[targetDate, targetUser, safeUsed, now]]); } else { sheet.appendRow([targetDate, targetUser, safeUsed, now]); } } function appendEtriLog_(log) { const sheet = getOrCreateEtriSheet_(ETRI_LOG_SHEET_NAME, ETRI_LOG_HEADERS); const now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'Asia/Seoul', 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'); sheet.appendRow([ now, sanitizeEtriDateKey_(log.dateKey || getKoreaDateKey_()), sanitizeEtriKey_(log.requestId || ''), sanitizeEtriKey_(log.userKey || 'guest'), String(log.studentName || ''), String(log.phoneLast4 || ''), String(log.script || '').slice(0, 1000), String(log.recognized || '').slice(0, 1000), String(log.score || ''), String(log.status || ''), String(log.message || '').slice(0, 1000) ]); } /**************************************************** * 31-2. ETRI 공통 유틸 ****************************************************/ function resultEtriCacheKey_(requestId) { return 'ETRI_PRON_RESULT_' + sanitizeEtriKey_(requestId); } function jsonpOutput_(e, obj) { const callback = e && e.parameter && e.parameter.callback ? String(e.parameter.callback).replace(/[^0-9A-Za-z_.$]/g, '') : ''; const json = JSON.stringify(obj); if (callback) { return ContentService .createTextOutput(callback + '(' + json + ');') .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT); } return jsonOutput_(obj); } // JSONP 또는 일반 JSON 응답 공통 출력 // - GitHub Pages/PWA에서는
